                <div n="13" type="level2" subtype="adhyāyaḥ">
                    <head> trayodaśo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
                    <l xml:id="Su.6.13.1"><label>ut.13.1</label> athāto lekhyarogapratiṣedhaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.13.2"><label>ut.13.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.13.3"><label>ut.13.3</label> nava ye 'bhihitā lekhyāḥ
                        sāmānyasteṣvayaṃ vidhiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         snigdhavāntaviriktasya nivātātapasadmani || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.13.4"><label>ut.13.4</label> (āptairdṛḍhaṃ gṛhītasya
                        veśmanyuttānaśāyinaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ) sukhodakaprataptena vāsasā susamāhitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         svedayed vartma nirbhujya vāmāṅguṣṭhāṅgulishtitam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.13.5"><label>ut.13.5</label> aṅgulyaṅguṣṭhakābhyāṃ tu nirbhugnaṃ
                        vartma yatnataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                        <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>plotāntarābhyāṃ na
                        yathā calati sraṃsate 'pi vā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.13.6"><label>ut.13.6</label> tataḥ pramṛjya plotena vartma
                        śastrapadāṅkitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         likhec chastreṇa patrair vā tato rakte sthite punaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.13.7"><label>ut.13.7</label> svinnaṃ
                            manohvākāsīsavyoṣārdrāñjanasaindhavaiḥ<ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref> |
                        <caesura/>
                         ślakṣṇapiṣṭaiḥ samākṣīkaiḥ pratisāryoṣṇavāriṇā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.13.8"><label>ut.13.8</label> prakṣālya haviṣā siktaṃ vraṇavat
                        samupācaret |
                        <caesura/>
                         svedāvapīḍaprabhṛtīṃstryahādūrdhvaṃ prayojayet || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.13.9"><label>ut.13.9</label> vyāsataste samuddiṣṭaṃ vidhānaṃ
                        lekhyakarmaṇi |
                        <caesura/>
                         asṛgāsrāvarahitaṃ kaṇḍūśophavivarjitam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.13.10"><label>ut.13.10</label> samaṃ nakhanibhaṃ vartma likhitaṃ
                        samyag iṣyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         raktamakṣi sravet skannaṃ kṣatācchastrakṛtāddhruvam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.13.11"><label>ut.13.11</label> rāgaśophaparisrāvāstimiraṃ
                        vyādhyanirjayaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vartma śyāvaṃ guru stabdhaṃ kaṇḍūharṣopadehavat || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.13.12"><label>ut.13.12</label> netrapākamudīrṇaṃ vā
                        kurvītāpratikāriṇaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         etaddurlikhitaṃ jñeyaṃ snehayitvā punarlikhet || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.13.13"><label>ut.13.13</label> vyāvartate yadā vartma pakṣma
                        cāpi <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>vimuhyati |
                        <caesura/>
                         syāt saruk srāvabahulaṃ tadatisrāvitaṃ viduḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.13.14"><label>ut.13.14</label> snehasvedādiriṣṭaḥ syāt
                        kramastatrānilāpahaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vartmāvabandhaṃ kliṣṭaṃ ca bahalaṃ yacca kīrtitam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.13.15"><label>ut.13.15</label> pothakīś cāpy avalikhet
                        pracchayitvāgrataḥ śanaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         samaṃ likhettu medhāvī śyāvakardamavartmanī || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.13.16"><label>ut.13.16</label> kumbhīkinīṃ śarkarāṃ ca
                        tathaivotsaṅginīm api |
                        <caesura/>
                        <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>kalpayitvā tu śastreṇa
                        likhet paścād atandritaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.13.17"><label>ut.13.17</label> bhaveyurvartmasu ca yāḥ piḍakāḥ
                        kaṭhinā bhṛśam |
                        <caesura/>
                         hrasvāstāmrāś ca tāḥ pakvā bhindyādbhinnā likhedapi || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.13.18"><label>ut.13.18</label> taruṇīś cālpasaṃrambhā piḍakā
                        bāhyavartmajāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         viditvaitāḥ praśamayet svedālepanaśodhanaiḥ ||</l>


                    <trailer>iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate śālākyatantre
                        lekhyarogapratiṣedho nāma trayodaśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||13 ||</trailer>

                <div n="14" type="level2" subtype="adhyāyaḥ">
                    <head>caturdaśo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
                    <l xml:id="Su.6.14.1"><label>ut.14.1</label> athāto bhedyarogapratiṣedhaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.14.2"><label>ut.14.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.14.3"><label>ut.14.3</label> svedayitvā bisagranthiṃ
                        chidrāṇyasya nirāśayam<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         pakvaṃ bhittvā tu śastreṇa sindhavenāvacūrṇayet || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.14.4"><label>ut.14.4</label> kāsīsamāgadhīpuṣpanepālyelāyutena
                        tu |
                        <caesura/>
                         tataḥ kṣaudraghṛtaṃ dattvā samyag bandhamathācaret || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.14.5"><label>ut.14.5</label> rocanākṣāratutthāni pippalyaḥ
                        kṣaudrameva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         pratisāraṇamekaikaṃ bhinne lagaṇa iṣyate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.14.6"><label>ut.14.6</label> mahaty api ca yuñjīta kṣārāgnī
                        vidhikovidaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         svinnāṃ bhinnāṃ viniṣpīḍya bhiṣagañjananāmikām || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.14.7"><label>ut.14.7</label> śilailānatasindhūtthaiḥ sakṣaudraiḥ
                        pratisārayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         rasāñjanamadhubhyāṃ tu bhittvā vā śastrakarmavit || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.14.8"><label>ut.14.8</label>
                        pratisāryāñjanairyuñjyāduṣṇairdīpaśikhodbhavaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         samyaksvinne kṛmigranthau bhinne syāt pratisāraṇam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.14.9"><label>ut.14.9</label> triphalātutthakāsīsasaindhavaiś ca
                            rasakriyā<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref> |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhittvopanāhaṃ kaphajaṃ pippalīmadhusaindhavaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.14.10"><label>ut.14.10</label> lekhayenmaṇḍalāgreṇa samantāt
                        pracchayed api |
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃsnehya patrabhaṅgaiś ca svedayitvā yathāsukham || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.14.11"><label>ut.14.11</label> sarveṣveteṣu vihitaṃ vidhānaṃ
                        snehapūrvakam |
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃpakve prayato bhūtvā kurvīta vraṇaropaṇam ||</l>


                    <trailer>iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate śālākyatantre

                <div n="15" type="level2" subtype="adhyāyaḥ">
                    <head>pañcadaśo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
                    <l xml:id="Su.6.15.1"><label>ut.15.1</label> athātaś chedyarogapratiṣedhaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.15.2"><label>ut.15.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.15.3"><label>ut.15.3</label> snigdhaṃ bhuktavato
                        hyannamupaviṣṭasya yatnataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃroṣayettu nayanaṃ bhiṣak cūrṇais tu lāvaṇaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.15.4"><label>ut.15.4</label> tataḥ saṃroṣitaṃ tūrṇaṃ susvinnaṃ
                        paridhaṭṭitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         arma yatra valījātaṃ tatraitallagayed bhiṣak || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.15.5"><label>ut.15.5</label> apāṅgaṃ prekṣamāṇasya baḍiśena
                        samāhitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         mucuṇḍyādāya medhāvī sūcīsūtreṇa vā punaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.15.6"><label>ut.15.6</label> na cotthāpayatā kṣipraṃ
                            kāryamabhyunnataṃ<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>
                        tu tat |
                        <caesura/>
                        <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>śastrābādhabhayāccāsya
                        vartmanī grāhayed dṛḍham || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.15.7"><label>ut.15.7</label> tataḥ praśithilībhūtaṃ tribhir eva
                        vilambitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         ullikhanmaṇḍalāgreṇa tīkṣṇena pariśodhayet || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.15.8"><label>ut.15.8</label> vimuktaṃ sarvataś cāpi
                        kṛṣṇācchuklācca maṇḍalāt |
                        <caesura/>
                         nītvā kanīnakopāntaṃ chindyānnātikanīnakam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.15.9"><label>ut.15.9</label> caturbhāgasthite māṃse nākṣi
                        vyāpattimṛcchati |
                        <caesura/>
                         kanīnakavadhādasraṃ nāḍī vāpyupajāyate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.15.10"><label>ut.15.10</label> hīnacchedāt punarvṛddhiṃ
                        śīgramevādhigacchati |
                        <caesura/>
                         arma yajjālavadvyāpi tadapyunmārjya<ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                            >&#x2020;</ref> lambitam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.15.11"><label>ut.15.11</label> chindyādvakreṇa śastreṇa
                        vartmaśuklāntamāthitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         pratisāraṇamakṣṇos tu tataḥ kāryamanantaram || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.15.12"><label>ut.15.12</label> yāvanālasya cūrṇena
                        trikaṭorlavaṇasya ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         svedayitvā tataḥ paś cādbadhnīyāt kuśalo bhiṣak || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.15.13"><label>ut.15.13</label> doṣartubalakālajñaḥ snehaṃ dattvā
                        yathāhitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         vraṇavat saṃvidhānaṃ tu tasya kuryād ataḥ param || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.15.14"><label>ut.15.14</label> tryahānmuktvā karasvedaṃ dattvā
                        śodhanamācaret |
                        <caesura/>
                         karañjabījāmalakamadhukaiḥ sādhitaṃ payaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.15.15"><label>ut.15.15</label> hitamāś cyotanaṃ śūle dvirahnaḥ
                        kṣaudrasaṃyutam |
                        <caesura/>

                         meṣasya puṣpairmadhukena saṃyutaṃ tadañjanaṃ sarvakṛte prayojayet || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.17.46"><label>ut.17.46</label> kriyāś ca sarvāḥ kṣatajodbhave
                        hitaḥ kramaḥ parimlāyini cāpi pittahṛt |
                        <caesura/>
                         kramo hitaḥ syandaharaḥ prayojitaḥ samīkṣya doṣeṣu<ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref> yathāsvam eva ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.17.47"><label>ut.17.47</label> doṣodaye naiva ca viplutiṃgate
                        dravyāṇi nasyādiṣu yojayed budhaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         punaś ca kalpe 'ñjanavistaraḥ śubhaḥ pravakṣyate 'nyastamapīha yojayet || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.17.48"><label>ut.17.48</label> ghṛtaṃ purāṇaṃ triphalāṃ
                        śatāvarīṃ paṭolamudgāmalakaṃ yavānapi |
                        <caesura/>
                         niṣevamāṇasya narasya yatnato bhayaṃ sughorarāttimirān na vidyate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.17.49"><label>ut.17.49</label> śatāvarīpāyasa eva kevalastathā

                         prabhūtasarpistriphalodakottaro yavaudano vā timiraṃ vyapohati || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.17.50"><label>ut.17.50</label> jīvantiśākaṃ suniṣaṇṇakaṃ ca

                        <caesura/>

                        paṭolakarkoṭakakāravellavārtākutarkārikarīrajāni |

                        <caesura/>
                         eraṇḍamūlaṃ ca samaṃ bṛhatyaṃśadvayānvitam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.18.104"><label>ut.18.104</label> ājena payasā piṣṭvā tāmrapātraṃ
                        pralepayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         saptakṛtvas tu tā vartyaś chāyāśuṣkā rujāpahāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.18.105"><label>ut.18.105</label>
                        pathyātutthakayaṣṭyāhvaistulyairmaricaṣoḍaśā |
                        <caesura/>
                         pathyā sarvavikāreṣu vartiḥ śītāmbupeṣitā || </l>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.19.3"><label>ut.19.3</label> abhyāhate tu nayane bahudhā narāṇāṃ

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.19.4"><label>ut.19.4</label> dṛṣṭiprasādajananaṃ vidhimāśu

                        <caesura/>

                        || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.19.5"><label>ut.19.5</label> sadyohate nayana eṣa

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.19.6"><label>ut.19.6</label> sādhyaṃ kṣataṃ paṭalamekamubhe tu

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.19.7"><label>ut.19.7</label> vistīrṇadṛṣṭitanurāgamasatpradarśi

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.19.8"><label>ut.19.8</label> netre vilambini vidhirvihitaḥ

                         ṣaṭsaptatirnayanajā ya ime pradiṣṭā rogā bhavantyamahatāṃ mahatāṃ ca

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.19.9"><label>ut.19.9</label>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.19.10"><label>ut.19.10</label> sūryaprabhāṃ na sahate sravati

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.19.11"><label>ut.19.11</label> taṃ vāmayettu

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.19.12"><label>ut.19.12</label> syātpippalīlavaṇamākṣikasaṃyutair

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.19.13"><label>ut.19.13</label> jambvāmradhātryaṇudalaiḥ

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.19.15"><label>ut.19.15</label> vyoṣaṃ palāṇḍu madhukaṃ

                    <head> viṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
                    <l xml:id="Su.6.20.1"><label>ut.20.1</label> athātaḥ
                        karṇagatarogavijñānīyamadhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.20.2"><label>ut.20.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.20.3"><label>ut.20.3</label> karṇaśūlaṃ praṇādaś ca bādhiryaṃ
                        kṣveḍa eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         karṇasrāvaḥ karṇakaṇḍūḥ karṇavarcas tathaiva ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.20.4"><label>ut.20.4</label> kṛmikarṇapratināhau
                        vidradhirdvividhastathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         karṇapākaḥ pūtikarṇastathaivārśaś caturvidham || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.20.5"><label>ut.20.5</label> karṇārbudaṃ saptavidhaṃ śophaś cāpi
                        caturvidhaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ete karṇagatā rogā aṣṭāviṃśatirīritāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.20.6"><label>ut.20.6</label> samīraṇaḥ śrotragato 'nyathācaraḥ
                        samantataḥ śūlamatīva karṇayoḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         karoti doṣaiś ca yathāsvamāvṛtaḥ sa karṇaśūlaḥ kathito durācaraḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.20.7"><label>ut.20.7</label> yadā tu nāḍīṣu vimārgamāgataḥ sa
                        eva śabdābhivahāsu tiṣṭhati |
                        <caesura/>
                         śrṇoti śabdān vividhāṃstadā naraḥ praṇādamenaṃ kathayanti cāmayam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.20.8"><label>ut.20.8</label> sa eva śabdānuvahā yadā sirāḥ
                        kaphānuyāto vyanusṛtya tiṣṭhati |
                        <caesura/>
                         tadā narasyāpratikārasevino bhavettu bādhiryamasaṃśayaṃ khalu || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.20.9"><label>ut.20.9</label> śramāt kṣayādrūkṣakaṣāyabhojanāt
                        samīraṇaḥ śabdapathe pratiṣṭhitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         viriktaśīrṣasya ca śītasevinaḥ karoti hi kṣveḍamatīva karṇayoḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.20.10"><label>ut.20.10</label> śirobhighātādathavā nimajjato
                        jale prapākādayavāpi vidradheḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sravettu pūyaṃ śravaṇo 'nilāvṛtaḥ sa karṇasaṃsrāva iti prakīrtitaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.20.11"><label>ut.20.11</label> kaphena kaṇḍūḥ pracitena
                        karṇayorbhṛśaṃ bhavet srotasi karṇasaṃjñite |
                        <caesura/>
                         viśoṣite śleṣmaṇi pittatejasā nṛṇāṃ bhavet srotasi karṇagūthakaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.20.12"><label>ut.20.12</label> sa karṇaviṭko dravatāṃ yadā gato
                        vilāyito ghrāṇamukhaṃ prapadyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         tadā sa karṇapratināhasaṃjñito bhavedvikāraḥ śiraso 'bhitāpanaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.20.13"><label>ut.20.13</label> yadā tu mūrcchantyathavāpi
                        jantavaḥ sṛjantyapatyānyathavāpi makṣikāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tadañjanatvācchravaṇo nirucyate bhiṣagbhir ādyaiḥ kṛmikarṇako gadaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.20.14"><label>ut.20.14</label> kṣatābhighātaprabhavastu
                        vidradhirbhavettathā doṣakṛto 'paraḥ punaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         saraktapītāruṇamasramāsravet pratodadhūmāyanadāhacopavān || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.20.15"><label>ut.20.15</label> bhavet prapākaḥ khalu pittakopato
                        vikothavikledakaraś ca karṇayoḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sthite kaphe srotasi pittatejasaḥ vilāyyamāne bhṛśasaṃpratāpavān || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.20.16"><label>ut.20.16</label> avedano vāpyathavā savedano
                        ghanaṃ sravet pūti ca pūtikarṇakaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pradiṣṭaliṅgānyaraśāṃsi tattvatas tathaiva śophārbudaliṅgamīritam |
                        <caesura/>
                         mayā purastāt prasamīkṣya yojayed ihaiva tāvat prayato bhiṣagvaraḥ ||</l>

                        <caesura/>
                         tīkṣṇā mūrdhavirekāś ca kavalāś cātra pūjitāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.21.34"><label>ut.21.34</label> karṇaśūlavidhiḥ kṛtsnaḥ
                        pittaghnaḥ śoṇitāvṛte |
                        <caesura/>
                         śūlapraṇādabādhiryakṣveḍānāṃ tu prakīrtitam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.21.35"><label>ut.21.35</label> sāmānyato viśeṣeṇa<ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref> bādhirye pūraṇaṃ śṛṇu
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         gavāṃ mūtreṇa bilvāni piṣṭvā tailaṃ vipācayet || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.21.36"><label>ut.21.36</label> sajalaṃ ca sadugdhaṃ ca bādhirye
                        karṇapūraṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         sitāmadhukabimbībhiḥ siddhaṃ vāje payasyapi || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.21.37"><label>ut.21.37</label> bimbīkvāthe vimathyoṣṇaṃ
                        śītībhūtaṃ taduddhṛtam |
                        <caesura/>
                         punaḥ paceddaśakṣīraṃ sitāmadhukacandanaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.21.38"><label>ut.21.38</label> bilvāmbugāḍhaṃ tattailaṃ bādhirye
                        karṇapūraṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         vakṣyate yaḥ pratiśyāye vidhiḥ so 'pyatra pūjitaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.21.39"><label>ut.21.39</label> vātavyādhiṣu yaś cokto vidhiḥ sa
                        ca hito bhavet |
                        <caesura/>
                         karṇasrāve pūtikarṇe tathaiva kṛmikarṇake || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.21.40"><label>ut.21.40</label> samānaṃ karma kurvīta yogān
                        vaiśeṣikānapi |
                        <caesura/>
                         śirovirecanaṃ caiva dhūpanaṃ pūraṇaṃ tathā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.21.41"><label>ut.21.41</label> pramārjanaṃ dhāvanaṃ ca vīkṣya
                        vīkṣyāvcārayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         rājavṛkṣāditoyena surasādigaṇena vā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.21.42"><label>ut.21.42</label> karṇaprakṣālanaṃ kāryaṃ
                        cūrṇaireṣāṃ ca pūraṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         kvāthaṃ pañjcakaṣāyaṃ tu kapittharasayojitam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.21.43"><label>ut.21.43</label> karṇasrāve praśaṃsanti pūraṇaṃ
                        madhunā saha |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarjatvakcūrṇasaṃyuktaḥ kārpāsīphalajo rasaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.21.44"><label>ut.21.44</label> yojito madhunā vāpi karṇasrāve
                        praśasyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         lākṣā rasāñjanaṃ sarjaś cūrṇitaṃ karṇapūraṇam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.21.45"><label>ut.21.45</label> saśaivalaṃ
                        mahāvṛkṣajambvāmraprasavāyutam |
                        <caesura/>
                         kulīrakṣaudramaṇḍūkīsiddhaṃ tailaṃ ca pūjitam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.21.46"><label>ut.21.46</label> tindukānyabhayā rodhraṃ
                        samaṅgāmalakaṃ madhu |
                        <caesura/>
                         pūraṇaṃ cātra<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref> pathyaṃ
                        syātkapittharasayojitam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.21.47"><label>ut.21.47</label> rasamāmrakapitthānāṃ
                        madhūkadhavaśālajam |
                        <caesura/>
                         pūraṇārthaṃ praśaṃsanti tailaṃ vā tairvipācitam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.21.48"><label>ut.21.48</label>
                        priyaṅgumadhukāmbaṣṭhādhātakīśilaparṇibhiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         mañjiṣṭhālobhralākṣābhiḥ kapitthasya rasena vā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.21.49"><label>ut.21.49</label> pacettailaṃ tadāsrāvamavagṛhṇāti
                        pūraṇāt |
                        <caesura/>
                         ghṛtaṃ rasāñjnaṃ nāryāḥ kṣīreṇa madhusaṃyutam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.21.50"><label>ut.21.50</label> tatpraśastaṃ cirotthe 'pi sāsrāve
                        pūtikarṇake |
                        <caesura/>
                         nirguṇḍīsvarasastailaṃ sindhurdhūmarajo guḍaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.21.51"><label>ut.21.51</label> pūraṇaḥ pūtikarṇasya śamano
                        madhusaṃyutaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṛmikarṇakanāśārthaṃ kṛmighnaṃ yojayed vidhim || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.21.52"><label>ut.21.52</label> vārtākudhūmaś ca hitaḥ
                        sārṣapasneha eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṛmighnaṃ haritālena gavāṃ mūtrayutena ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.21.53"><label>ut.21.53</label> gugguloḥ karṇadaurgandhye
                        dhūpanaṃ śreṣṭhamucyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         chardanaṃ dhūmapānaṃ ca kavalasya ca dhāraṇam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.21.54"><label>ut.21.54</label> karṇakṣveḍe hitaṃ tailaṃ sārṣapaṃ
                        caiva pūraṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         vidradhau cāpi kurvīta vidradhyuktaṃ cikitsitam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.21.55"><label>ut.21.55</label> prakledya dhīmāṃstailena svedena
                        pravilāyya ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         śodhayetkarṇaviṭkaṃ tu bhiṣak samyak śalākayā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.21.56"><label>ut.21.56</label> nāḍīsvedo 'tha vamanaṃ dhūmo
                        mūrdhavirecanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         vidhiś ca kaphahṛtsarvaḥ karṇakaṇḍūmapohati || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.21.57"><label>ut.21.57</label> atha karṇapratīnāhe snehasvedau
                        prayojayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         tato viriktaśirasaḥ kriyāṃ prāptāṃ samācaret || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.21.58"><label>ut.21.58</label> karṇapākasya bhaiṣajyaṃ
                        kuryātpittavisarpavat |
                        <caesura/>
                         karṇacchidre vartamānaṃ kīṭaṃ kledamalādi vā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.21.59"><label>ut.21.59</label> śṛṅgeṇāpahareddhīmānathavāpi
                        śalākayā |
                        <caesura/>
                         śeṣāṇāṃ tu vikārāṇāṃ prāk cikitsitamīritam ||</l>


                    <trailer>iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate śālākyatantre
                        karṇagatarogapratiṣedho nāmaikaviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||21 ||</trailer>

                <div n="22" type="level2" subtype="adhyāyaḥ">
                    <head>dvāviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||</head>
                    <l xml:id="Su.6.22.1"><label>ut.22.1</label> athāto
                        nāsāgatarogavijñānīyamadhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.22.2"><label>ut.22.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.22.3"><label>ut.22.3</label> apīnasaḥ pūtinasyaṃ<ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref> nāsāpākas tathaiva ca
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         tathā śoṇitapittaṃ ca pūyaśoṇitam eva ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.22.4"><label>ut.22.4</label> kṣavathurbhraṃśathurdīpto nāsānāhaḥ
                        parisravaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         nāsāśoṣeṇa sahitā daśaikāś ceritā gadāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.22.5"><label>ut.22.5</label> catvāryarśāṃsi catvāraḥ śophāḥ
                        saptārbudāni ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         pratiśyāyāś ca ye pañca vakṣyante sacikitsitāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                        <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>ekatriṃśanmitāste tu
                        nāsārogāḥ prakīrtitāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.22.6"><label>ut.22.6</label> ānahyate yasya vidhūpyate ca
                        praklidyate śuṣyati<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>
                        cāpi nāsā |
                        <caesura/>
                         na vetti yo gandharasāṃś ca janturjuṣṭaṃ vyavasyettamapīnasena || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.22.7"><label>ut.22.7</label> taṃ cānilaśleṣmabhavaṃ vikāraṃ
                        brūyāt pratiśyāyasamānaliṅgam |
                        <caesura/>
                         doṣairvidagdhairlatālumūle saṃvāsito yasya samīraṇas tu || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.22.8"><label>ut.22.8</label> nireti pūtirmukhanāsikābhyāṃ taṃ
                        pūtināsaṃ pravadanti rogam |
                        <caesura/>
                         vrāṇāśritaṃ pittamarūṃṣi kuryād yasmin vikāre balavāṃś ca pākaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.22.9"><label>ut.22.9</label> taṃ nāsikāpākam iti vyavasyed
                        vikledakothāvapi yatra dṛṣṭau |
                        <caesura/>
                         caturvidhaṃ dviprabhavaṃ vakṣyāmi bhūyaḥ khalu raktapittam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.22.10"><label>ut.22.10</label> doṣairvidagdhairathavāpi
                        jantorlalāṭadeśe 'bhihatasya tais tu |
                        <caesura/>
                         nāsā sravet pūyamasṛgvimiśraṃ taṃ pūyaraktaṃ pravadanti rogam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.22.11"><label>ut.22.11</label> ghrāṇāśrite marmaṇi
                            saṃpraduṣṭe<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>
                        yasyānilo nāsikayā nireti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.22.12"><label>ut.22.12</label> kaphānuyāto bahuśaḥ saśabdastaṃ
                        rogamāhuḥ kṣavathuṃ vidhijñāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tīkṣṇopayogādatijighrato vā bhāvān kaṭūnarkanirīkṣaṇādvā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.22.13"><label>ut.22.13</label> sūtrādibhir vā
                        taruṇāsthimarmaṇyudghāṭite 'nyaḥ kṣavathurnireti |
                        <caesura/>
                         prabhraśyate nāsikayaiva yaś ca<ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                            >&#x2020;</ref> sāndro vidagdho lavaṇaḥ kaphas tu || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.22.14"><label>ut.22.14</label> prāk saṃcito mūrdhani
                        pittataptastaṃ bhraṃśathuṃ vyādhimudāharanti |
                        <caesura/>
                         ghrāṇe bhṛśaṃ dāhasamanvite tu viniḥsareddhūma iveha vāyuḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.22.15"><label>ut.22.15</label> nāsā pradīpteva ca yasya
                        jantorvyādhiṃ tu taṃ dīptamudāharanti |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaphāvṛto vāyurudānasaṃjño yadā svamārge viguṇaḥ sthitaḥ syāt || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.22.16"><label>ut.22.16</label> ghrāṇaṃ vṛṇotīva tadā sa rogo
                        nāsāpratīnāha iti pradiṣṭaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ajasramacchaṃ salilaprakāśaṃ yasyāvivarṇe sravatīha nāsā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.22.17"><label>ut.22.17</label> rātrau viśeṣeṇa hi taṃ vikāraṃ
                        nāsāparisrāvam iti vyavasyet |
                        <caesura/>
                         ghrāṇāśrite śleṣmaṇi mārutena pittena gāḍhaṃ pariśoṣite ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.22.18"><label>ut.22.18</label> samucchvasityūrdhvamadhaś ca
                        kṛcchrādyastasya nāsāpariśoṣa uktaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         doṣaiśtribhistaiḥ pṛthagekaśaś ca brūyāttathārśāṃsi tathaiva śophān || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.22.19"><label>ut.22.19</label> śālākyasiddhāntamavekṣya cāpi
                        sarvātmakaṃ saptamamarbudaṃ tu |
                        <caesura/>
                         rogaḥ pratiśyāya ihopadiṣṭaḥ sa vakṣyate pañcavidhaḥ purastāt || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.22.20"><label>ut.22.20</label> (nāsāsrotogatā rogāstriṃśadekaś
                        ca kīrtitāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         srotaḥpathe yadvipulaṃ kośavaccārbudaṃ bhavet<ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref> ||) </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.22.21"><label>ut.22.21</label> śophās tu śophavijñānā
                        nāsāsrotovyavasthitāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         nidāne 'rśāṃsi nirdiṣṭānyevaṃ tāni vibhāvayet ||</l>


                    <trailer>iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate śālākyatantre
                        nāsāgatarogavijñānīyo nāma dvāviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||22 ||</trailer>

                <div n="23" type="level2" subtype="adhyāyaḥ">
                    <head>trayoviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
                    <l xml:id="Su.6.23.1"><label>ut.23.1</label> athāto nāsāgatarogapratiṣedhaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.23.2"><label>ut.23.2</label> athovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.23.3"><label>ut.23.3</label> pūrvoddiṣṭe pūtinasye ca jantoḥ
                        snehasvedau chardanaṃ sraṃsanaṃ ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         yuktaṃ bhaktaṃ tīkṣṇamalpaṃ laghu syāduṣṇaṃ toyaṃ dhūmapānaṃ ca kāle || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.23.4"><label>ut.23.4</label> hiṅgu vyoṣaṃ vatsakākhyaṃ śivāṭī
                        lākṣā bījaṃ saurabhaṃ kaṭphalaṃ ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         ugrā kuṣṭhaṃ tīkṣṇagandhā viḍaṅgaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ nityaṃ cāvapīḍe karañjam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.23.5"><label>ut.23.5</label> etairdravyaiḥ sārṣapaṃ mūtrayuktaṃ
                        tailaṃ dhīmānnasyahetoḥ paceta |
                        <caesura/>
                         nāsāpāke pittahṛtsaṃvidhānaṃ kāryaṃ sarvaṃ bāhyamābhyantaraṃ ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.23.6"><label>ut.23.6</label> hṛtvā raktaṃ kṣīravṛkṣatvacaś ca
                        sājyāḥ sekā yojanīyāś ca lepāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vakṣyāmyūrdhvaṃ raktapītopaśāntiṃ nāḍīvatsyāt pūyarakte cikitsā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.23.7"><label>ut.23.7</label> vānte samyak cāvapīḍaṃ vadanti
                        tīkṣṇaṃ dhūmaṃ śodhanaṃ cātra nasyam |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣepyaṃ nasyaṃ mūrdhavairecanīyairnāḍyā cūrṇaṃ kṣavathau bhraṃśathau ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.23.8"><label>ut.23.8</label> kuryāt svedān mūrdhni vātāmayaghnān
                        snigdhān dhūmān yadyanyaddhitaṃ ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         dīpte roge paittikaṃ saṃvidhānaṃ kuryāt sarvaṃ svādu yacchītalaṃ ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.23.9"><label>ut.23.9</label> nāsānāhe snehapānaṃ pradhānaṃ
                        snigdhā dhūmā mūrdhabastiś ca nityam |
                        <caesura/>
                         balātailaṃ sarvathaivopayojyaṃ vātavyādhāvanyaduktaṃ ca yadyat || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.23.10"><label>ut.23.10</label> nāsāsrāve ghrāṇataś cūrṇamuktaṃ
                        nāḍyā deyaṃ yo 'vapīḍaś ca tīkṣṇaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tīkṣṇaṃ dhūmaṃ devadārvagnikābhyāṃ māṃsaṃ vājaṃ yuktamatrādiśanti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.23.11"><label>ut.23.11</label> nāsāśoṣe kṣīrasarpiḥ pradhānaṃ
                        siddhaṃ tailaṃ cāṇukalpena nasyam |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarpiḥpānaṃ bhojanaṃ jāṅgalaiś ca snehaḥ svedaḥ snaihikaś cāpi dhūmaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.23.12"><label>ut.23.12</label> śeṣān rogān ghrāṇajān
                        sanniyaccheduktaṃ teṣāṃ yadyathā saṃvidhānam ||</l>


                    <trailer>iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate śālākyatantre
                        nāsāgatarogapratiṣedho nāma trayoviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||23 ||</trailer>
                </div>
                <div n="24" type="level2" subtype="adhyāyaḥ">
                    <head>caturviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
                    <l xml:id="Su.6.24.1"><label>ut.24.1</label> athātaḥ pratiśyāyapratiṣedhaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.24.2"><label>ut.24.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.24.3"><label>ut.24.3</label> nārīprasaṅgaḥ śiraso 'bhitāpo dhūmo
                        rajaḥ śītamatipratāpaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃdhāraṇaṃ mūtrapurīṣayoś ca sadyaḥ pratiśyāyanidānamuktam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.24.4"><label>ut.24.4</label> cayaṃ gatā mūrdhani mārutādayaḥ
                        pṛthak samastāś ca tathaiva śoṇitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         prakopyamāṇā vividhaiḥ prakopaṇairnṛṇāṃ pratiśyāyakarā bhavanti hi || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.24.5"><label>ut.24.5</label> śirogurutvaṃ kṣavathoḥ pravartanaṃ
                        tathāṅgamardaḥ parihṛṣṭaromatā |
                        <caesura/>
                         upadravāś cāpy apare pṛthagvidhā nṛṇāṃ pratiśyāyapuraḥsarāḥ smṛtāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.24.6"><label>ut.24.6</label> ānaddhā pihitā nāsā
                        tanusrāvapravartinī |
                        <caesura/>
                         galatālvoṣṭhaśoṣaś ca nistodaḥ śaṅkhayostathā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.24.7"><label>ut.24.7</label> svaropaghātaś ca bhavet pratiśyāye
                        'nilātmake |
                        <caesura/>
                         uṣṇaḥ sapītakaḥ srāvo ghrāṇāt sravati paittike || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.24.8"><label>ut.24.8</label> kṛśo 'tipāṇḍuḥ santapto
                        bhavettṛṣṇānipīḍitaḥ(tṛṣṇābhipīḍitaḥ) |
                        <caesura/>
                         sadhūmaṃ sahasā vahniṃ vamatīva ca mānavaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.24.9"><label>ut.24.9</label> kaphaḥ kaphakṛte ghrāṇācchuklaḥ
                        śītaḥ sravenmuhuḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śuklāvabhāsaḥ śūnākṣo bhavedguruśiromukhaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.24.10"><label>ut.24.10</label> śirogalauṣṭhatālūnāṃ
                        kaṇḍūyanamatīva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhūtvā bhūtvā pratiśyāyo yo 'kasmādvinivartate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.24.11"><label>ut.24.11</label> saṃpakvo vāpyapakvo vā sa
                        sarvaprabhavaḥ smṛtaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         liṅgāni caiva sarveṣāṃ pīnasānāṃ ca sarvaje || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.24.12"><label>ut.24.12</label> raktaje tu pratiśyāye raktāsrāvaḥ
                        pravartate |
                        <caesura/>
                         tāmrākṣaś ca bhavejjantururoghātaprapīḍitaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.24.13"><label>ut.24.13</label> durgandhocchvāsavadanastathā
                        gandhān na vetti ca |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.26.27"><label>ut.26.27</label> nasye hi śoṇitaṃ dadyāttena
                        mūrcchanti jantavaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         mattāḥ śoṇitagandhena samāyānti yatastataḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.26.28"><label>ut.26.28</label> teṣāṃ nirharaṇaṃ kāryaṃ tato
                        mūrdhavirecanaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         hrasvaśigrukabījair vā kāṃsyanīlīsamāyutaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.26.29"><label>ut.26.29</label> kṛmighnairavapīḍaiś ca
                        mūtrapiṣṭairupācaret |
                        <caesura/>
                         pūtimatsyayutān dhūmān kṛmighnāṃś ca prayojayet || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.26.30"><label>ut.26.30</label> bhojanāni kṛmighnāni pānāni
                        vividhāni ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         sūryāvarte vidhātavyaṃ nasyakarmādibheṣajam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.26.31"><label>ut.26.31</label> bhojanaṃ jāṅgalaprāyaṃ
                        kṣīrānnavikṛtirghṛtam |
                        <caesura/>
                         tathārdhabhedake vyādhau prāptamanyacca yadbhavet || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.26.32"><label>ut.26.32</label> śirīṣamūlakaphalairavapīḍo
                        'nayorhitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vaṃśamūlakaphalairavapīḍo 'nayorhitaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.26.33"><label>ut.26.33</label> avapīḍo hitaś cātra
                        vacāmāgadhikāyutaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         madhukenāvpīḍo vā madhunā saha saṃyutaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.26.34"><label>ut.26.34</label> manaḥśilāvapīḍo vā madhunā
                        candanena vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         teṣāmante hitaṃ nasyaṃ sarpirmadhurasānvitam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.26.35"><label>ut.26.35</label> sārivotpalakuṣṭhāni madhukaṃ
                        cāmlapeṣitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarpistailayuto lepo dvayorapi sukhāvahaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.26.36"><label>ut.26.36</label> eṣa eva prayoktavyaḥ śiroroge
                        kaphātmake |
                        <caesura/>
                         anantavāte kartavyaḥ sūryāvartaharo<ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                            >&#x2020;</ref> vidhiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.26.37"><label>ut.26.37</label> sirāvyadhaś ca kartavyo
                        'nantavātapraśāntaye |
                        <caesura/>
                         āhāraś ca vidhātavyo vātapittavināśanaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.26.38"><label>ut.26.38</label> madhumastakasaṃyāvaghṛtapūraiś ca
                        bhojanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣīrasarpiḥ praśaṃsanti nasye pāne ca śaṅkhake || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.26.39"><label>ut.26.39</label> jāṅgalānāṃ rasaiḥ
                        snigdhairāhāraś cātra śasyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         śatāvarīṃ tilān kṛṣṇān madhukaṃ nīlamutpalam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.26.40"><label>ut.26.40</label> dūrvāṃ punarnavāṃ caiva lepe
                        sādhvavacārayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         mahāsugandhāmathavā pālindīṃ cāmlapeṣitām || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.26.41"><label>ut.26.41</label> śītāṃś cātra parīṣekān pradehāṃś ca
                        prayojayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         avapīḍaś ca deyo 'tra sūryāvartanivāraṇaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.26.42"><label>ut.26.42</label> kṛmikṣayakṛtau hitvā śirorogeṣu
                        buddhimān |
                        <caesura/>
                         madhutailasamāyuktaiḥ śirāṃsyativirecayet || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.26.43"><label>ut.26.43</label> paś cātsarṣapatailena tato nasyaṃ
                        prayojayet |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.26.44"><label>ut.26.44</label> paś cādupācaretsamyak sirāṇāmatha
                        mokṣaṇaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ṣaṭsaptatirnetrarogā daśāṣṭādaśa karṇajāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.26.45"><label>ut.26.45</label> ekatriṃśad ghrāṇagatāḥ
                        śirasyekādaśaiva tu |
                        <caesura/>
                         iti vistarato dṛṣṭāḥ(diṣṭāḥ) salakṣaṇacikitsitāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.26.46"><label>ut.26.46</label> etāvanto
                        yathāsthūlamuttamāṅgagatā gadāḥ |

                    <head>saptaviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
                    <l xml:id="Su.6.27.1"><label>ut.27.1</label> athāto
                        navagrahākṛtivijñānīyamadhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.27.2"><label>ut.27.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.27.3"><label>ut.27.3</label> bālagrahāṇāṃ vijñānaṃ sādhanaṃ cāpy
                        anantaram |
                        <caesura/>
                         utpattiṃ kāraṇaṃ caiva suśrutaikamanāḥ śṛṇu || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.27.4"><label>ut.27.4</label> skandagrahas tu prathamaḥ
                        skandāpasmāra eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         śakunī revatī caiva pūtanā cāndhapūtanā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.27.5"><label>ut.27.5</label> pūtanā śītanāmā ca tathaiva
                        mukhamaṇḍikā |
                        <caesura/>
                         navamo naigameṣaś ca yaḥ pitṛgrahasaṃjñitaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.27.6"><label>ut.27.6</label> dhātrīmātroḥ
                        prākpradiṣṭāpacārācchaucabhraṣṭānmaṅgalācārahīnān |
                        <caesura/>
                         trastān hṛṣṭāṃtarjitān tāḍitān vā pūjāhetorhiṃsyurete kumārān || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.27.7"><label>ut.27.7</label> aiśvaryasthāste na śakyā viśanto
                        dehaṃ draṣṭuṃ mānuṣairviśvarūpāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         āptaṃ vākyaṃ tatsamīkṣyābhidhāsye liṅgānyeṣāṃ yāni dehe bhavanti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.27.8"><label>ut.27.8</label> śūnākṣaḥ<ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref> kṣatajasagandhikaḥ
                        stanadviḍ vakrāsyo hatacalitaikapakṣmanetraḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         udvigraḥ sululitacakṣuralparodī skandārto bhavati ca gāḍhamuṣṭivarcāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.27.9"><label>ut.27.9</label> niḥsaṃjño bhavati
                        punarbhavetsasaṃjñaḥ saṃrabdhaḥ karacaraṇaiś ca nṛtyatīva |
                        <caesura/>
                         viṇmūtre sṛjati vinadya jṛmbhamāṇaḥ phenaṃ ca prasṛjati tatsakhābhipannaḥ
                        || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.27.10"><label>ut.27.10</label> srastāṅgo bhayacakito
                        vihaṅgagandhiḥ saṃsrāvivraṇaparipīḍitaḥ samantāt |
                        <caesura/>
                         sphoṭaiś ca pracitatanuḥ sadāhapākairvijñeyo bhavati śiśuḥ kṣataḥ śakunyā
                        || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.27.11"><label>ut.27.11</label> raktāsyo haritamalo 'tipāṇḍudehaḥ
                        śyāvo vā jvaramukhapākavedanātaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         revatyā viyathitatanuś ca karṇanāsaṃ mṛdgāti dhruvamabhipīḍitaḥ kumāraḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.27.12"><label>ut.27.12</label> srastāṅgaḥ svapiti sukhaṃ divā na
                        rātrau viḍ bhinnaṃ sṛjati ca kākatulyagandhiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         chardyārto hṛṣitatanūruhaḥ kumārastṛṣṇālurbhavati ca pūtanāgṛhītaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.27.13"><label>ut.27.13</label> yo dveṣṭi
                        stanamatisārakāsahikkācchardībhir jvarasahitābhir ardyamānaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         durvarṇaḥ satatamadhaḥśayo 'mlagandhistaṃ brūyurbhiṣaja ihāndhapūtanārtam
                        || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.27.14"><label>ut.27.14</label> udvigro bhṛśamativepate prarudyāt
                        saṃlīnaḥ ssvapiti ca yasya cāntrakūjaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         visrāṅgo bhṛśamatisāryate ca yastaṃ jānīyādbhiṣagiha śītapūtanārtam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.27.15"><label>ut.27.15</label> mlānāṅgaḥ surucirapāṇipādavaktro
                        bahvāśī kaluṣasirāvṛtodaro yaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sodvego bhavati ca mūtratulyagandhiḥ sa jñeyaḥ śiśuriha vaktramaṇḍikārtaḥ
                        || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.27.16"><label>ut.27.16</label> yaḥ phenaṃ vamati vinamyate ca
                        madhye sodvegaṃ vilapati cordhvamīkṣamāṇaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         jvaryeta pratatamatho vasāsagandhirniḥsaṃjño bhavati hi naigameṣajuṣṭaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.27.17"><label>ut.27.17</label> prastabdho yaḥ stanadveṣī muhyate
                        cāviśanmuhuḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         taṃ bālamacirāddhanti grahaḥ saṃpūrṇalakṣaṇaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.27.18"><label>ut.27.18</label> viparītamataḥ sādhyaṃ
                        cikitsedacirārditam |
                        <caesura/>
                         gṛhe purāṇahaviṣābhyajya bālaṃ śucau śuciḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.27.19"><label>ut.27.19</label> sarṣapān prakiretteṣāṃ
                            tailairdīpaṃ<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref> ca
                        kārayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         sadā sannihitaṃ cāpi juhuyāddhavyavāhanam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.27.20"><label>ut.27.20</label>
                        sarvagandhauṣadhībījairgandhamālyairalaṅkṛtam |
                        <caesura/>
                         agnye kṛttikābhyaś ca svāhā svāheti saṃtatam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.27.21"><label>ut.27.21</label> namaḥ skandāya devāya
                        grahādhipataye namaḥ |
                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>
                         nīrujo nirvikāraś ca śiśurme jāyatāṃ drutam ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.30.1"><label>ut.30.1</label> athātaḥ śakunīpratīṣedhaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.30.2"><label>ut.30.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.30.3"><label>ut.30.3</label> śakunyabhiparītasya kāryo vaidyena
                        jānatā |
                        <caesura/>
                         vetasāmrakapitthānāṃ niṣkvāthaḥ pariṣecane || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.30.4"><label>ut.30.4</label> kaṣāyamadhurais tailaṃ
                        kāryamabhyañjane śiśoḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         madhukośīrahrīberasārivotpalapadmakaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.30.5"><label>ut.30.5</label> rodhrapriyaṅgumañjiṣṭhāgairikaiḥ
                        pradihec chiśum |
                        <caesura/>
                         vraṇeṣūktāni cūrṇāni pathyāni vividhāni ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.30.6"><label>ut.30.6</label> skandagrahe dhūpanāni tānīhāpi
                        prayojayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         śatāvarīmṛgairvārunāgadantīnidigdhikāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.30.7"><label>ut.30.7</label> lakṣmaṇāṃ sahadevāṃ ca bṛhatīṃ cāpi
                        dhārayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         tilataṇḍulakaṃ mālyaṃ haritālaṃ manaḥśilā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.30.8"><label>ut.30.8</label> balirepa karañjeṣu nivedyo
                        niyatātmanā |
                        <caesura/>
                         niṣkuṭe ca prayoktavyaṃ snānamasya yathāvidhi || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.30.9"><label>ut.30.9</label> skandāpasmāraśamanaṃ ghṛtaṃ cāpīha
                        pūjitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         kuryāc ca vividhāṃ pūjāṃ śakunyāḥ kusumaiḥ śubhaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.30.10"><label>ut.30.10</label> antarīkṣacarā devī
                        sarvālaṅkārabhūṣitā |
                        <caesura/>
                         ayomukhī tīkṣṇatuṇḍā śakunī te prasīdatu || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.30.11"><label>ut.30.11</label> durdarśanā mahākāyā piṅgākṣī
                        bhairavasvarā |
                        <caesura/>
                         lambodarī <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>śaṅkukarṇī
                        śakunī te prasīdatu ||</l>


                    <trailer>iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kumāratantre
                        śakunīpratiṣedho nāma (caturtho 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) triṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||30
                        ||</trailer>
                </div>

                    <head>ekatriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
                    <l xml:id="Su.6.31.1"><label>ut.31.1</label> athāto revatīpratiṣedhaṃ

                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.31.4"><label>ut.31.4</label> tailamabhyañjane kāryaṃ kuṣṭhe

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.31.6"><label>ut.31.6</label> kulatthāḥ śaṅkhacūrṇaṃ ca pradehaḥ

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.31.7"><label>ut.31.7</label> sandhyayorubhayoḥ
                        kāryametaduddhūpanaṃ śiśoḥ |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.31.8"><label>ut.31.8</label> satataṃ dhārayeccāpi kṛtaṃ vā

                        prayatātmanā |

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.31.10"><label>ut.31.10</label> nānāvastradharā devī

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.31.11"><label>ut.31.11</label> upāsate yāṃ satataṃ devyo

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>
                         revatī śuṣkanāmā yā sā te devī prasīdatu ||</l>


                    <trailer>iti suśurtasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kumāratantre

                <div n="37" type="level2" subtype="adhyāyaḥ">
                    <head>saptatriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
                    <l xml:id="Su.6.37.1"><label>ut.37.1</label> athāto grahotpattimadhyāyaṃ

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.37.2"><label>ut.37.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.37.3"><label>ut.37.3</label> nava skandādayaḥ proktā bālānāṃ ya
                        ime grahāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śrīmanto divyavapuṣo nārīpuruṣavigrahāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.37.4"><label>ut.37.4</label> ete guhasya rakṣārthaṃ
                        kṛttikomāgniśūlibhiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sṛṣṭāḥ śaravaṇasthasya rakṣitasyātmatejasā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.37.5"><label>ut.37.5</label> strīvigrahā grahā ye tu nānārūpā
                        mayeritāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         gaṅgomākṛttikānāṃ te bhāgā rājasatāmasāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.37.6"><label>ut.37.6</label> naigameṣas tu pārvatyā sṛṣṭo
                        meṣānano grahaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kumāradhārī devasya guhasyātmasamaḥ sakhā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.37.7"><label>ut.37.7</label> skandāpasmārasaṃjño yaḥ so
                        'gnināgnisamadyutiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sa ca skandasakhā nāma viśākha iti cocyate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.37.8"><label>ut.37.8</label> skandaḥ sṛṣṭo bhagavatā devena
                        tripurāriṇā |
                        <caesura/>
                         bibharti cāparāṃ saṃjñāṃ kumāra iti sa grahaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.37.9"><label>ut.37.9</label> bālalīlādharo yo 'yaṃ devo
                        rudrāgnisṃbhavaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         mithyācāreṣu<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref> bhagavān
                        svayaṃ naiṣa pravartate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.37.10"><label>ut.37.10</label> kumāraḥ skandasāmānyādatra
                        kecidapaṇḍitāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         gṛhṇātītyalpavijñānā bruvate dehacintakāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.37.11"><label>ut.37.11</label> tato bhagavati skande
                        surasenāpatau kṛte |
                        <caesura/>
                         upatasthurgrahāḥ sarve dīptaśaktidharaṃ guham || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.37.12"><label>ut.37.12</label> ūcuḥ prāñjalayaś cainaṃ vṛttiṃ
                        naḥ saṃvidhatsva vai |
                        <caesura/>
                         teṣāmarthe tataḥ skandaḥ śivaṃ devamacodayat || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.37.13"><label>ut.37.13</label> tato grahāṃstānuvāca bhagavān
                        bhaganetrahṛt |
                        <caesura/>
                         tiryagyoniṃ mānuṣaṃ ca tritayaṃ jagat || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.37.14"><label>ut.37.14</label> parasparopakāreṇa vartate
                        dhāryate 'pi ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         devā manuṣyān prīṇanti tairyagyonīṃs tathaiva ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.37.15"><label>ut.37.15</label> vartamānairyathākālaṃ
                        śītavarṣoṣṇamārutaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ijyāñjalinamaskārajapahomavratādibhiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.37.16"><label>ut.37.16</label> narāḥ samyak prayuktaiś ca
                        prīṇanti tridiveśvarān |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhāgadheyaṃ vibhaktaṃ ca śeṣaṃ kiñcin na vidyate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.37.17"><label>ut.37.17</label> tadyuṣmākaṃ śubhā vṛttirbāleṣveva
                        bhaviṣyati |
                        <caesura/>
                         kuleṣu yeṣu nejyante devāḥ pitara eva ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.37.18"><label>ut.37.18</label> brāhmaṇāḥ sādhavaś caiva guravo
                        'tithayastathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         nivṛttācāraśauceṣu parapākopajīviṣu || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.37.19"><label>ut.37.19</label> utsannabalibhikṣeṣu
                        bhinnakāṃsyopabhojiṣu |
                        <caesura/>
                         gṛheṣu teṣu ye bālāstān gṛhṇīdhvamaśaṅkitāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.37.20"><label>ut.37.20</label> tatra vo vipulā vṛttiḥ pūjā caiva
                        bhaviṣyati |
                        <caesura/>
                         evaṃ grahāḥ samutpannā bālān gṛhṇanti cāpy ataḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.37.21"><label>ut.37.21</label> grahopasṛṣṭā bālāstu
                        duś cikitsyatamā matāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vaikalyaṃ maraṇaṃ cāpi dhruvaṃ skandagrahe matam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.37.22"><label>ut.37.22</label> skandagraho 'tyugratamaḥ
                        sarveṣveva yataḥ smṛtaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         anyo vā sarvarūpas tu na sādhyo graha ucyate ||</l>


                    <trailer>iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kumāratantre

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.38.6"><label>ut.38.6</label> jāyante bījadoṣācca daivācca śṛṇu

                         yato 'maratvaṃ saṃprāptāstridaśāstridiveśvarāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.39.40"><label>ut.39.40</label> sāsro nirbhugnahṛdayo<ref

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.39.115"><label>ut.39.115</label> (tīkṣṇe jvare gurau dehe

                         madhurāmlaiḥ śṛtaṃ tailaṃ sarpirvāpyanuvāsanam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.40.109"><label>ut.40.109</label> gudapākas tu pittena yasya

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.40.110"><label>ut.40.110</label> dadhimaṇḍasurābilvasiddhaṃ

                    <head>ekacatvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
                    <l xml:id="Su.6.41.1"><label>ut.41.1</label> athātaḥ śoṣapratiṣedhaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.41.3"><label>ut.41.3</label> anekarogānugato bahurogapurogamaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         durvijñeyo durnivāraḥ śoṣo vyādhirmahābalaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.41.4"><label>ut.41.4</label> saṃśoṣaṇādrasādīnāṃ śoṣa

                        <caesura/>
                         cayāpacayavān vṛttaḥ sa gulma iti kīrtitaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.42.5"><label>ut.42.5</label> pañca gulmāśrayā nṝṇāṃ pārśve

                        <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                        >&#x2020;</ref>gupitānilamūlatvādgūḍhamūlodayādapi || </l>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.42.7"><label>ut.42.7</label> antaḥ sarati yasmācca na
                        pākamupayātyataḥ |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.42.8"><label>ut.42.8</label> puruṣāṇāṃ tathā strīṇāṃ jñeyo
                        raktena cāparaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sadanaṃ madantā vahnerāṭopo 'ntravikūjanam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.42.9"><label>ut.42.9</label> viṇmūtrānilasaṅgaś ca
                        sauhityāsahatā tathā |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.42.10"><label>ut.42.10</label> hṛtkukṣiśūlaṃ mukhakaṇṭhaśoṣo
                        vāyornirodho viṣamāgnitā ca |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.42.11"><label>ut.42.11</label>
                        svedajvarāhāravidāhadāhāstṛṣṇāṅgarāgaḥ kaṭuvaktratā ca |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.42.12"><label>ut.42.12</label> staimityamanne
                        'ruciraṅgasādaś chardiḥ praseko madhurāsyatā ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaphasya liṅgāni ca yāni tāni bhavanti gulme kaphasaṃbhave tu || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.42.13"><label>ut.42.13</label> sarvātmakaḥ sarvavikārayuktaḥ so
                        'sādhya uktaḥ kṣatajaṃ pravakṣye |
                        <caesura/>
                         navaprasūtāhitabhojanā yā yā cāmagarbhaṃ visṛjedṛtau<ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref> vā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.42.14"><label>ut.42.14</label> vāyurhi tasyāḥ parigṛhya raktaṃ
                        karoti gulmaṃ sarujaṃ sadāham |
                        <caesura/>
                         paittasya liṅgena samānaliṅgaṃ viśeṣaṇaṃ cāpy aparaṃ nibodha || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.42.15"><label>ut.42.15</label> na spandate nodarameti vṛddhiṃ
                        bhavanti liṅgāni ca garbhiṇīnām |
                        <caesura/>
                         taṃ garbhakālātigame caikitsyamasṛgbhavaṃ gulmamuśanti tajjñāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.42.16"><label>ut.42.16</label> vātagulmārditaṃ snigdhaṃ yuktaṃ
                        snehavirecanaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         upācaredyathākālaṃ nirūhaiḥ sānuvāsanaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.42.17"><label>ut.42.17</label> pittagulmārditaṃ snigdhaṃ

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.42.97"><label>ut.42.97</label> madhvāsavena cukreṇa
                        surāsauvīrakeṇa vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         athavaitāni(athacaitāni) cūrṇāni mātuluṅgarasena vā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.42.98"><label>ut.42.98</label> tathā badarayūṣeṇa bhāvitāni
                        punaḥ punaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tāni hiṅgupragāḍhāni saha śarkarayā pibet || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.42.99"><label>ut.42.99</label> saha dāḍimasāreṇa vartiḥ kāryā
                        bhiṣagjitā |
                        <caesura/>
                         sā vartirvātikaṃ śūlaṃ kṣiprameva vyapohati || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.42.100"><label>ut.42.100</label> guḍatailena vā līḍhā pītā
                        madyena vā punaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         bubhukṣāprabhave śūle laghu saṃtarpaṇaṃ hitam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.42.101"><label>ut.42.101</label> uṣṇaiḥ kṣīrairyavāgūbhiḥ

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.42.102"><label>ut.42.102</label> susaṃskṛtāḥ pradeyāḥ

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.42.103"><label>ut.42.103</label> etadvātasamutthasya śūlasyoktaṃ

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.42.104"><label>ut.42.104</label> sa sukhaṃ chardayitvā tu pītvā
                        śītodakaṃ naraḥ |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.42.105"><label>ut.42.105</label> maṇirājatatāmrāṇi bhājanāni ca

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.42.106"><label>ut.42.106</label> guḍaḥ śāliryavāḥ kṣīraṃ

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.42.107"><label>ut.42.107</label> rasān seveta pittaghnān

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.42.108"><label>ut.42.108</label> parūṣakāṇi

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.42.109"><label>ut.42.109</label> aśane bhuktamātre tu prakopaḥ

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.42.110"><label>ut.42.110</label> rūkṣaḥ svedaḥ prayojyaḥ
                        syādanyāś coṣṇāḥ kriyā hitāḥ |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.42.111"><label>ut.42.111</label> pāṭhāṃ vacāṃ trikaṭukaṃ tathā

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.42.112"><label>ut.42.112</label> eraṇḍaphalamūlāni mūlaṃ

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.42.114"><label>ut.42.114</label> etat saṃbhṛtya saṃbhāraṃ

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.42.118"><label>ut.42.118</label> sa saṃruddhaḥ karotyāśu <ref

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.42.137"><label>ut.42.137</label> śūlaṃ saṃjanayaṃstīvraṃ

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.42.143"><label>ut.42.143</label> avipākagataṃ hyannaṃ śūlaṃ
                        tīvraṃ karotyati |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.42.144"><label>ut.42.144</label> viricyate chardayati kampate
                        'tha vimuhyati |
                        <caesura/>
                         avipākād bhavec chūlas tv annadoṣasamudbhavaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.42.145"><label>ut.42.145</label> vamanaṃ laṅghanaṃ svedaḥ
                        pācanaṃ phalavartayaḥ |
                        <caesura/>

                        śasyante śūlanāśanāḥ || gulmāvasthāḥ kriyāḥ kāryā yathāvat sarvaśūlinām
                        ||</l>

                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.43.3"><label>ut.43.3</label>
                        vegāghātoṣṇarūkṣānnairatimātropasevitaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         viruddhādhyaśanājīrṇairasātmyaiś cāpi(cāti) bhojanaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.43.4"><label>ut.43.4</label> dūṣayitvā rasaṃ doṣā viguṇā hṛdayaṃ
                        gatāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kurvanti hṛdaye bādhāṃ hṛdrogaṃ taṃ pracakṣate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.43.5"><label>ut.43.5</label> caturvidhaḥ sa doṣaiḥ syāt
                            kṛmibhiś ca<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref> pṛthak
                        pṛthak |
                        <caesura/>
                         lakṣaṇaṃ tasya vakṣyāmi cikitsitamanantaram || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.43.6"><label>ut.43.6</label> āyamyate mārutaje hṛdayaṃ <ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>tudyate tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         nirmathyate dīryate ca sphoṭyate pāṭyate 'pi ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.43.7"><label>ut.43.7</label> tṛṣṇoṣādāhacoṣāḥ syuḥ paittike
                        hṛdayaklamaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         dhūmāyanaṃ ca mūrcchā ca svedaḥ śoṣo mukhasya ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.43.8"><label>ut.43.8</label> gauravaṃ kaphasaṃsrāvo 'ruciḥ
                        stambho 'gnimārdavam |
                        <caesura/>
                         mādhuryam api cāsyasya balāsāvatate hṛdi || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.43.9"><label>ut.43.9</label> utkleśaḥ ṣṭhīvanaṃ todaḥ śūlo
                        hṛllāsakastamaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         aruciḥ śyāvnetratvaṃ śoṣaś ca kṛmije bhavet || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.43.10"><label>ut.43.10</label> bhramaklamau sādaśoṣau
                        jñeyāsteṣāmupadravāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṛmije kṛmijātīnāṃ ślaiṣmikāṇāṃ ca ye matāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.43.11"><label>ut.43.11</label> vātopasṛṣṭe hṛdaye vāmayet

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.43.12"><label>ut.43.12</label> pippalyelāvacāhiṅguyavabhasmāni

                        phaladhānyāmlakaulatthadadhimadyāsavādibhiḥ |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.43.14"><label>ut.43.14</label> bhojayejjīrṇaśālyannaṃ jāṅgalaiḥ

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.43.15"><label>ut.43.15</label>
                        śrīparṇīmadhukakṣaudrasitotpalajalairvamet |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.43.16"><label>ut.43.16</label> ghṛtaṃ kaṣāyāṃś coddiṣṭān

                         tṛptasya ca rasairmukhyairmadhuraiḥ<ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                            >&#x2020;</ref> saghṛtairbhiṣak || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.43.17"><label>ut.43.17</label> sakṣaudraṃ <ref

                        <caesura/>
                         vacānimbakaṣāyābhyāṃ vāntaṃ hṛdi kaphātmake || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.43.18"><label>ut.43.18</label> cūrṇaṃ tu pāyayetoktaṃ vātaje
                            bhojayecca<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref> tam |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.43.19"><label>ut.43.19</label> śyāmātrivṛtkalkayutaṃ ghṛtaṃ vāpi

                        <caesura/>
                        <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>balātailairvidadhyāc
                        ca bastiṃ bastiviśāradaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.43.20"><label>ut.43.20</label> kṛmihṛdrogiṇaṃ snigdhaṃ bhojayet
                        piśitaudanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         dadhnā ca palalopetaṃ tryahaṃ paś cādvirecayet || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.43.21"><label>ut.43.21</label> sugandhibhiḥ salavaṇairyogaiḥ
                        sājājiśarkaraiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         viḍaṅgagāḍhaṃ dhānyāmlaṃ pāyayetāpyanantaram || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.43.22"><label>ut.43.22</label> hṛdayasthāḥ patantyevamadhastāt
                        krimayo nṛṇām |
                        <caesura/>
                         yavānnaṃ vitareccāsya saviḍaṅgamataḥ param ||</l>

                <div n="44" type="level2" subtype="adhyāyaḥ">
                    <head>catuś catvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
                    <l xml:id="Su.6.44.1"><label>ut.44.1</label> athātaḥ pāṇḍurogapratiṣedhaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.44.2"><label>ut.44.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvandariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.44.3"><label>ut.44.3</label> vyavāyamamlaṃ lavaṇāni madyaṃ mṛdaṃ
                        divāsvapnamatīva tīkṣṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         niṣevamāṇasya vidūṣya raktaṃ kurvanti doṣāstvaci pāṇḍubhāvam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.44.4"><label>ut.44.4</label> pāṇḍvāmayo 'ṣṭārdhavidhaḥ pradiṣṭaḥ
                        pṛthaksamastairyugapacca doṣaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarveṣu caiteṣviha pāṇḍubhāvo yato 'dhiko 'taḥ khalu pāṇḍurogaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.44.5"><label>ut.44.5</label> tvaksphoṭanaṃ ṣṭhīvanagātrasādau
                        mṛdbhakṣaṇaṃ prekṣaṇakūṭaśothaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         viṇmūtrapītatvamathāvipāko bhaviṣyatastasya puraḥsarāṇi || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.44.6"><label>ut.44.6</label> sa kāmalāpānakipāṇḍurogaḥ
                        kumbhāhvayo lāgharako(lāghavako)+alasākhyaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vibhāṣyate lakṣaṇamasya kṛtsnaṃ nibodha vakṣyāmyanupūrvaśastat<ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref> || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.44.7"><label>ut.44.7</label> kṛṣṇekṣaṇaṃ kṛṣṇasirāvanaddhaṃ
                        tadvarṇaviṇmūtranakhānanaṃ ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         vātena pāṇḍuṃ manujaṃ vyavasyed yuktaṃ tathānyais tadupadravaiś ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.44.8"><label>ut.44.8</label> pītekṣaṇaṃ pītasirāvanaddhaṃ
                        tadvarṇaviṇmūtranakhānanaṃ ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         pittena pāṇḍuṃ manujaṃ vyavasyed yuktaṃ tathānyais tadupadravaiś ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.44.9"><label>ut.44.9</label> śuklekṣaṇaṃ śuklasirāvanaddhaṃ
                        tadvarṇaviṇmūtranakhānanaṃ ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaphena pāṇḍuṃ manujaṃ vyavasyed yuktaṃ tathānyais tadupadravaiś ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.44.10"><label>ut.44.10</label> sarvātmake sarvam idaṃvyavasyed
                        vakṣyāmi liṅgānyatha kāmalāyāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yo hyāmayānte sahasānnamamlamadyādapathyāni ca tasya pittam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.44.11"><label>ut.44.11</label> karoti pāṇḍuṃ vadanaṃ viśeṣāt
                            <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>pūrveritau
                        tandribalakṣayau ca |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.44.12"><label>ut.44.12</label>
                        jvarāṅgamardabhramasādatandrākṣayānvito lāgharako(lāghavako)+alasākhyaḥ |
                        <caesura/>

                        >&#x2020;</ref>vātapittāddharipītanīlaṃ halīmakaṃ nāma vadanti tajjñāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.44.13"><label>ut.44.13</label> upadravāsteṣvaruciḥ pipāsā

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.44.14"><label>ut.44.14</label> sādhyaṃ tu pāṇḍvāmayinaṃ samīkṣya

                        <caesura/>
                         saṃpādayet kṣaudraghṛtapragāḍhairharītakīcūrṇayutaiḥ prayogaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.44.15"><label>ut.44.15</label> pibedghṛtaṃ vā rajanīvipakvaṃ

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.44.16"><label>ut.44.16</label> mūtre nikumbhārdhapalaṃ vipācya

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.44.17"><label>ut.44.17</label> ayorajovyoṣaviḍaṅgacūrṇaṃ

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.44.18"><label>ut.44.18</label> ahrecca doṣān bahuśo 'lpamātrān

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.44.19"><label>ut.44.19</label> ubhe bṛhatyau rajanīṃ śukākhyāṃ

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.44.20"><label>ut.44.20</label> tat pāṇḍutāṃ hantyupayujyamānaṃ

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.44.22"><label>ut.44.22</label> ājaṃ śakṛtsyāt<ref

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.44.24"><label>ut.44.24</label> bibhītakāyomalanāgarāṇāṃ cūrṇaṃ

                        <caesura/>
                        <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>takrānupāno vaṭakaḥ

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.44.25"><label>ut.44.25</label> sauvarcalaṃ hiṅgu kirātatiktaṃ

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.44.34"><label>ut.44.34</label> lauhaṃ ca kiṭṭaṃ bahuśaś ca
                        taptvā nirvāpya mūtre bahuśas tathaiva |
                        <caesura/>
                         ekīkṛtaṃ gojalapiṣṭametadaikadhyamāvāpya pacedukhāyām || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.44.35"><label>ut.44.35</label> yathā na dahyeta tathā viśuṣkaṃ

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.44.36"><label>ut.44.36</label> drākṣāguḍūcyāmalakīrasaiś ca

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.44.38"><label>ut.44.38</label>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.44.39"><label>ut.44.39</label> anteṣu śūnaṃ parihīnamadhyaṃ
                        mlānaṃ tathānteṣu ca madhyaśūnam |

                         gude ca śephasyatha muṣkaśūnaṃ<ref rend="superscript footnote marker"

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.44.40"><label>ut.44.40</label> vivarjayet pāṇḍukinaṃ yaśo 'rthī

                        daurbalyaśvāsakāsajvaravamathumadāstandritādāhamūrcchā bhukte cānne

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.45.29"><label>ut.45.29</label> palāśavṛkṣasvarase vipakvaṃ
