                        <caesura/>
                         vanaspatīnāṃ svarasaiḥ kṛtaṃ vā saśarkaraṃ kṣīraghṛtaṃ pibedvā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.45.30"><label>ut.45.30</label> drākṣāmuśīrāṇyatha padmakaṃ sitā
                        pṛthakpalāṃśānyudake samāvapet |
                        <caesura/>
                         sthitaṃ niśāṃ tadrudhirāmayaṃ jayet pītaṃ payo vāmbusamaṃ hitāśinaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.45.31"><label>ut.45.31</label> turaṅgavarcaḥsvarasaṃ samākṣikaṃ
                        pibet sitākṣaudrayutaṃ vṛṣasya vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         lihettathā vāstukabījacūrṇaṃ kṣaudrānvitaṃ taṇḍulasāhvayaṃ vā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.45.32"><label>ut.45.32</label> lihyāc ca lājāñjanacūrṇamekamevaṃ
                        sitākṣaudrayutāṃ tugākhyām |
                        <caesura/>
                         drākṣāṃ sitāṃ tiktakarohiṇīṃ ca himāmbunā vā madhukena yuktām || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.45.33"><label>ut.45.33</label> pathyāmahiṃsrāṃ rajanīṃ ghṛtaṃ ca
                        lihyāttathā śoṇitapittarogī |
                        <caesura/>
                         vāsākaṣāyotpalamṛtpriyaṅgurodhrāñjanāmbhoruhakeśarāṇi || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.45.34"><label>ut.45.34</label> pītvā sitākṣaudrayutāni jahyāt
                        pittasṛjo vegamudīrṇamāśu |
                        <caesura/>
                         gāyatrijambvarjunakovidāraśirīṣarodhrāśanaśālmalīnām || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.45.35"><label>ut.45.35</label> puṣpāṇi śigroś ca vicūrṇya leho
                        madhvanvitaḥ śoṇitapittaroge |
                        <caesura/>
                         sakṣaudramindīvarabhasmavāri karañjabījaṃ <ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>madhusarpiṣī ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.45.36"><label>ut.45.36</label> jambvarjunāmrakvathitaṃ ca toyaṃ
                        ghnanti trayaḥ pittamasṛk ca yogāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         mūlāni puṣpāṇi ca mātuluṅgyāḥ piṣṭvā pibettaṇḍuladhāvanena || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.45.37"><label>ut.45.37</label> ghrāṇapravṛtte jalamāśu deyaṃ
                        saśarkaraṃ nāsikayā payo vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         drākṣārasaṃ kṣīraghṛtaṃ pibedvā saśarkaraṃ cekṣurasaṃ himaṃ vā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.45.38"><label>ut.45.38</label> śītopacāraṃ madhuraṃ ca
                        kuryād viśeṣataḥ śoṇitapittaroge |
                        <caesura/>
                         drākṣāghṛtakṣaudrasitāyutena vidārigandhādivipācitena || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.45.39"><label>ut.45.39</label> kṣīreṇa cāsthāpanamagryamuktaṃ
                        hitaṃ ghṛtaṃ cāpy anuvāsanārtham |
                        <caesura/>
                         priyaṅgurodhrāñjanagairikotpalaiḥ suvarṇakālīyakaraktacandanaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.45.40"><label>ut.45.40</label>
                        sitāśvagandhāmbudayaṣṭikāhvayairmṛṇālasaugandhikatulyapeṣitaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         nirūhya cainaṃ payasā samākṣikairghṛtaplutaiḥ śītajalāvasecitam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.45.41"><label>ut.45.41</label> kṣīraudanaṃ bhuktamathānuvāsayed
                        ghṛtena yaṣṭīmadhusādhitena ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         adhovahaṃ śoṇitameṣa nāśayettathātisāraṃ rudhirasya dustaram || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.45.42"><label>ut.45.42</label> virekayoge tvati caiva śasyate
                        vāmyaś ca rakte vijite balānvitaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.45.43"><label>ut.45.43</label> evaṃvidhā uttarabāstayaś ca
                        mūtrāśayasthe rudhire vidheyāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pravṛttarakteṣu ca pāyujeṣu kuryād vidhānaṃ khalu raktapaittam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.45.44"><label>ut.45.44</label> vidhiś cāsṛgdare 'pyeṣa strīṇāṃ
                        kāryo vijānatā |
                        <caesura/>
                         śastrakarmaṇi raktaṃ ca yasyātīva pravartate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.45.45"><label>ut.45.45</label> trayāṇām api doṣāṇāṃ śoṇite 'pi
                        ca sarvaśaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         liṅgānyālokya kartavyaṃ cikitsitamanantaram ||</l>


                    <trailer>iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kāyacikitsātantre

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.46.17"><label>ut.46.17</label> bhujaṅgapuṣpaṃ maricānyuśīraṃ

                         śītena toyena<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref> bisaṃ

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.46.18"><label>ut.46.18</label> kuryāc ca nāsāvadanāvarodhaṃ
                        kṣīraṃ pibedvāpyatha mānuṣīṇām |
                        <caesura/>
                         mūrcchāṃ prasaktāṃ tu śirovirekairjayed abhīkṣṇaṃ vamanaiś ca tīkṣṇaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.46.19"><label>ut.46.19</label>
                        <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>harītakīkvāthaśṛtaṃ

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.46.20"><label>ut.46.20</label> pibet kaṣāyāṇi ca gandhavanti

                         prabhūtadoṣastamaso 'tirekāt saṃmūrcchito naiva vibudhyate yaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.46.21"><label>ut.46.21</label> saṃnyastasaṃjño bhṛśaduś cikitsyo

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.46.22"><label>ut.46.22</label> tadvaccikitsettvarayā

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.46.23"><label>ut.46.23</label>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.46.24"><label>ut.46.24</label> prabuddhasaṃjñaṃ
                        vamanānulomyaistīkṣṇairviśuddhaṃ laghupathyabhuktam |

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.47.3"><label>ut.47.3</label> madyamuṣṇaṃ tathā tīkṣṇaṃ sūkṣmaṃ

                        <caesura/>
                         rūkṣamāśukaraṃ caiva vyavāyi ca vikāśi ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.47.4"><label>ut.47.4</label> auṣṇyācchītopacāraṃ
                        tattaikṣṇyāddhanti manogatim |
                        <caesura/>
                         viśatyavayavān saukṣmyādvaiśadyātkaphaśukranut || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.47.5"><label>ut.47.5</label> mārutaṃ kopayed
                            raukṣyādāśutvāccāśukarmakṛt<ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                            >&#x2020;</ref> |
                        <caesura/>
                         harṣadaṃ ca vyavāyitvādvikāśitvādvisarpati || </l>

                        rocanadīpanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         kecillavaṇavarjyāṃs tu rasānatrādiśanti hi || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.47.7"><label>ut.47.7</label> snigdhais tadannairmāṃsaiś ca
                        bhakṣyaiś ca saha sevitam |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.47.8"><label>ut.47.8</label> kāmyatā manasastuṣṭirdhairyaṃ tejo
                        'tivikramaḥ |

                         vidhivat sevyamāne tu madye sannihitā guṇāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.47.9"><label>ut.47.9</label> tadevānannamajñena

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.47.10"><label>ut.47.10</label> madena karaṇānāṃ tu bhāvānyatve
                        kṛte sati |

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.47.14"><label>ut.47.14</label> nirbhaktamekāntata eva madyaṃ

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.47.17"><label>ut.47.17</label> pānātyayaṃ paramadaṃ
                        pānājīrṇamathāpi vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         pānavibhramamugraṃ ca teṣāṃ vakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.47.18"><label>ut.47.18</label>
                        stambhāṅgamardhṛdayagrahatodakampāḥ pānātyaye 'nilakṛte śiraso rujaś ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         svedapralāpamukhaśoṣaṇadāhamūrcchāḥ pittātmake vadanalocanapītatā ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.47.19"><label>ut.47.19</label> śleṣmātmake
                        vamathuśītakaphaprasekāḥ sarvātmake bhavati sarvavikārasaṃpat |
                        <caesura/>
                         ūṣmāṇamaṅgagurutāṃ virasānanatvaṃ śleṣmādhikatvamaruciṃ malamūtrasaṅgam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.47.20"><label>ut.47.20</label> liṅgaṃ parasya tu madasya vadanti
                        tajjñāstṛṣṇāṃ rujāṃ śirasi sandhiṣu cāpi bhedam |
                        <caesura/>
                         ādhmānamudgiraṇamamlaraso vidāho 'jīrṇasya pānajanitasya vadanti liṅgam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.47.21"><label>ut.47.21</label> jñeyāni tatra bhiṣajā
                        suviniś citāni pittaprakopajanitāni ca kāraṇāni |
                        <caesura/>
                         hṛdgātratodavamathujvarakaṇṭhadhūmamūrcchākaphasravaṇamūrdharujo vidāhaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.47.22"><label>ut.47.22</label> dveṣaḥ surānnavikṛteṣu ca teṣu
                        teṣu taṃ pānavibhramamuśantyakhilena dhīrāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         hīnottarauṣṭhamatiśītamamandadāhaṃ
                        tailaprabhāsyamatipānahataṃ(tailaprabhāsyamapipānahataṃ) vijahyāt || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.47.23"><label>ut.47.23</label> jihvauṣṭhadantamasitaṃ tvathavāpi
                        nīlaṃ pīte ca yasya nayane rudhiraprame ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         hikkājvarau vamathuvepathupārśvaśūlāḥ kāsabhramāvapi ca pānahataṃ bhajante
                        || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.47.24"><label>ut.47.24</label> teṣāṃ nivāraṇam idaṃhi
                        mayocyamānaṃ vyaktābhidhānamakhilena vidhiṃ nibodha |
                        <caesura/>
                         madyaṃ tu cukramaricārdrakadīpyakuṣṭhasauvarcalāyutamalaṃ<ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref> pavanasya śāntyai || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.47.25"><label>ut.47.25</label>
                        pṛthvīkadīpyakamahauṣadhahiṅgubhir vā sauvarcalena ca yutaṃ vitaret sukhāya
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         āmrātakāmraphaladāḍimamātuluṅgaiḥ kuryācchubhāny api ca ṣaḍavapānakāni || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.47.26"><label>ut.47.26</label> seveta vā phalarasopahitān
                        rasādīnānūpavargapiśitāny api gandhavanti |
                        <caesura/>
                         pittātmake madhuravargakaṣāyamiśraṃ madyaṃ hitaṃ samadhuśarkaramiṣṭagandham
                        || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.47.27"><label>ut.47.27</label> pītvā ca madyamapi
                        cekṣurasapragāḍhaṃ niḥśeṣataḥ kṣaṇamavasthitamullikhecca |
                        <caesura/>
                         lāvaiṇatittirirasāṃś ca pibedanamlān maudgān sukhāya saghṛtān sasitāṃś ca
                        yūṣān || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.47.28"><label>ut.47.28</label> pānātyaye kaphakṛte
                        kaphamullikhecca madyena bimbividulodakasaṃyutena |
                        <caesura/>
                         seveta tiktakaṭukāṃś ca rasānudārān yūṣāṃś ca tiktakaṭukopahitān hitāya || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.47.29"><label>ut.47.29</label> pathyaṃ yavānnavikṛtāni ca
                        jāṅgalāni śleṣmaghnamanyadapi yacca niratyayaṃ syāt |
                        <caesura/>
                         kuryāc ca sarvamatha sarvabhave vidhānaṃ ddvandvodbhave dvayamavekṣya
                        yathāpradhānam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.47.30"><label>ut.47.30</label> sāmānyamanyadapi yacca
                        samagramagryaṃ vakṣyāmi yacca manaso madakṛt sukhaṃ ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         tvaṅgāgapuṣpamagadhailamadhūkadhānyaiḥ ślakṣṇairajājimaricaiś ca kṛtaṃ
                        samāṃśaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.47.31"><label>ut.47.31</label> pānaṃ
                        kapittharasavāriparūṣakāḍhyaṃ pānātyayeṣu vidhivatsrutamambarānte |
                        <caesura/>
                         hrīverapadmaparipelavasaṃprayuktaiḥ puṣpairvilipya karavīrajalodbhavaiś ca
                        || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.47.32"><label>ut.47.32</label> piṣṭaiḥ sapadmakayutairapi
                        sārivādyaiḥ sekaṃ jalaiś ca vitaredamalaiḥ suśītaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tvakpatracocamaricailabhujaṅgapuṣpaśleṣmātakaprasavavalkaguḍairupetam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.47.33"><label>ut.47.33</label> drākṣāyutaṃ hṛtamalaṃ
                        madirāmayārtais tatpānakaṃ śuci sugandhi narairniṣevyam |
                        <caesura/>
                         piṣṭvā pibec ca madhukaṃ kaṭurohiṇīṃ ca drākṣāṃ ca mūlamasakṛt
                        trapuṣībhavaṃ yat || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.47.34"><label>ut.47.34</label>
                        <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>kārpāsinīmatha ca

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.47.35"><label>ut.47.35</label> tadbījapūrakarasāyutamāśu pītaṃ

                        <caesura/>

                        || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.47.36"><label>ut.47.36</label> sauvarcalāyutamudārarasaṃ
                        phalāmlaṃ bhārgīśṛtena ca jalena hito 'vasekaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.47.37"><label>ut.47.37</label> ikṣvākudhāmārgavavṛkṣakāṇi

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.47.38"><label>ut.47.38</label>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.47.39"><label>ut.47.39</label> hṛdyaiḥ khaḍair api ca

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.47.40"><label>ut.47.40</label>
                            kharjūravetrakakarīraparūṣakeṣu<ref rend="superscript footnote marker"

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.47.42"><label>ut.47.42</label> seveta vā

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.47.59"><label>ut.47.59</label> vāpīṃ bhajeta

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.48.1"><label>ut.48.1</label> athātastṛṣṇāpratiṣedhamadhyāyaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.48.2"><label>ut.48.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.48.3"><label>ut.48.3</label> satataṃ yaḥ pibedvāri na
                        tṛptimadhigacchati |
                        <caesura/>
                         punaḥ kāṅkṣati toyaṃ ca taṃ tṛṣṇārditamādiśet || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.48.4"><label>ut.48.4</label>
                        <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                            >&#x2020;</ref>sakṣobhaśokaśramamadyapānādrūkṣāmlaśuṣkoṣṇakaṭūpayogāt<ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref> |
                        <caesura/>
                         dhātukṣayāllaṅghanasūryatāpāt pittaṃ ca vātaś ca bhṛśaṃ pravṛddhau || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.48.5"><label>ut.48.5</label> srotāṃsi saṃdūṣayataḥ sametau
                        yānyambuvāhīni śarīriṇāṃ hi |
                        <caesura/>
                         srotaḥsvapāṃvāhiṣu dūṣiteṣu jāyeta tṛṣṇātibalā<ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref> tatas tu || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.48.6"><label>ut.48.6</label> tisraḥ smṛtāstāḥ kṣatajā caturthī
                        kṣayāttathānyāmasamudbhavā ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         syāt saptamī bhaktanimittajā tu nibodha<ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref> liṅgānyanupūrvaśastu
                        || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.48.7"><label>ut.48.7</label> tālvoṣṭhakaṇṭhāsyaviśoṣadāhāḥ<ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>
                        saṃtāpamohabhramavipralāpāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pūrvāṇi rūpāṇi bhavanti tāsāmutpattikāleṣu viśeṣatas tu || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.48.8"><label>ut.48.8</label> śuṣkāsyatā mārutasaṃbhavāyāṃ
                        todastathā <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                        >&#x2020;</ref>śaṅkhaśiraḥsu cāpi |
                        <caesura/>
                         srotonirodho virasaṃ ca vaktraṃ śītabhir adbhiś ca vivṛddhimeti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.48.9"><label>ut.48.9</label> mūrcchāpralāpārucivaktraśoṣāḥ
                        pītekṣaṇatvaṃ pratataś ca dāhaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śītābhikāṅkṣā mukhatiktatā ca pittātmikāyāṃ paridhūpanaṃ ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.48.10"><label>ut.48.10</label> kaphāvṛtābhyāmanilānalābhyāṃ
                        kapho 'pi śuṣkaḥ prakaroti tṛṣṇām<ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                            >&#x2020;</ref> |
                        <caesura/>
                         nidrā gurutvaṃ madhurāsyatā ca tayārditaḥ<ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref> śuṣyati cātimātram || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.48.11"><label>ut.48.11</label> kaṇṭhopalepo mukhapicchilatvaṃ
                        śītajvaraś chardirarocakaś ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaphātmikāyāṃ gurugātratā ca śākhāsu śophastvavipāka eva |
                        <caesura/>
                         etāni rūpāṇi bhavanti tasyāṃ tayārditaḥ kāṅkṣati nāti cāmbhaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.48.12"><label>ut.48.12</label> kṣatasya rukśoṇitanirgamābhyāṃ
                        tṛṣṇā caturthī kṣatajā <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                            >&#x2020;</ref>matā tu |
                        <caesura/>
                         tayābhibhūtasya niśādināni gacchanti duḥkhaṃ pibato 'pi toyam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.48.13"><label>ut.48.13</label>
                        <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>rasakṣayādyā kṣayajā
                        matā sā tayārditaḥ śuṣyati dahyate ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         atyarthamākāṅkṣati cāpi toyaṃ tāṃ sannipātāditi kecidāhuḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.48.14"><label>ut.48.14</label> rasakṣayoktāni ca lakṣaṇāni
                        tasyāmaśeṣeṇa bhiṣagvyavasyet |
                        <caesura/>
                         tridoṣaliṅgāmasamudbhavā ca hṛcchūlaniṣṭhīvanasādayuktā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.48.15"><label>ut.48.15</label> snigdhaṃ tathāmlaṃ lavaṇaṃ ca
                        bhuktaṃ <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                        >&#x2020;</ref>gurvannamevātitṛṣāṃ karoti |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣīṇaṃ vicittaṃ badhiraṃ tṛṣārtaṃ vivarjayennirgatajihvamāśu || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.48.16"><label>ut.48.16</label> tṛṣṇābhivṛddhāvudare ca pūrṇe taṃ
                        vāmayenmāgadhikodakena |
                        <caesura/>
                        <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>vilobhanaṃ cātra hitaṃ
                        vidheyaṃ syāddāḍimāmrātakamātuluṅgaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.48.17"><label>ut.48.17</label> tisraḥ prayogairiha sannivāryāḥ
                        śītaiś ca samyag rasavīryajātaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         gaṇḍūṣamamlairvirase ca vaktre kuryācchubhairāmalakasya cūrṇaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.48.18"><label>ut.48.18</label> suvarṇarūpyādibhir
                        agnitaptairloṣṭaiḥ kṛtaṃ vā sikatādibhir vā<ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref> |
                        <caesura/>
                         jalaṃ sukhoṣṇaṃ śamayettu tṛṣṇāṃ saśarkaraṃ kṣaudrayutaṃ himaṃ vā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.48.19"><label>ut.48.19</label> pañcāṅgikāḥ pañcagaṇā ya
                            uktāsteṣvambu<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>
                        siddhaṃ prathame gaṇe vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         pibet sukhoṣṇaṃ manujo<ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                            >&#x2020;</ref>+acireṇa tṛṣo vimucyeta hi vātajāyāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.48.20"><label>ut.48.20</label> pittaghnavargais tu kṛtaḥ kaṣāyaḥ
                        saśarkaraḥ kṣaudrayutaḥ suśītaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pītastṛṣāṃ pittakṛtāṃ nihanti kṣīraṃ śṛtaṃ vāpyatha jīvanīyaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.48.21"><label>ut.48.21</label>
                            bilvāḍhakīkanyakapañcamūlīdarbheṣu<ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref> siddhaṃ kaphajāṃ
                        nihanti |
                        <caesura/>
                         hitaṃ bhavec chardanameva cātra taptena nimbaprasavodakena || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.48.22"><label>ut.48.22</label> sarvāsu tṛṣṇāsvathavāpi paittaṃ
                        kuryād vidhiṃ tena<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref> hi
                        tā na santi |
                        <caesura/>
                         paryāgatodumbarajo rasas tu saśarkaratatkvathitodakaṃ vā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.48.23"><label>ut.48.23</label> vargasya siddhasya ca sārivādeḥ
                        pātavyamambhaḥ śiśiraṃ tṛṣārtaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaśeruśṛṅgāṭakapadmamocabisekṣusiddhaṃ<ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref> kṣatajāṃ nihanti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.48.24"><label>ut.48.24</label> lājotpalośīrakucandanāni dattvā
                        pravāte niśi vāsayettu |
                        <caesura/>
                         taduttamaṃ toyamudāragandhi sitāyutaṃ kṣaudrayutaṃ <ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>vadanti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.48.25"><label>ut.48.25</label> drākṣāpragāḍhaṃ ca hitāya
                        vaidyastṛṣṇārditebhyo vitarennarebhyaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sasārivādau tṛṇapañcamūle tathotpalādau <ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>prathame gaṇe ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.48.26"><label>ut.48.26</label> kuryāt kaṣāyaṃ ca yatheritena<ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref> madhūkapuṣpādiṣu
                        cāpareṣu |
                        <caesura/>
                         rājādanakṣīrikapītaneṣu ṣaṭ pānakānyatra hitāni ca syuḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.48.27"><label>ut.48.27</label> satuṇḍikerāṇyathavā pibettu
                        piṣṭāni kārpāsasamudbhavāni |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣatodbhavāṃ rugvinivāraṇena jayed rasānāmasṛjaś ca pānaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.48.28"><label>ut.48.28</label> kṣayotthitāṃ kṣīraghṛtaṃ
                        nihanyānmāṃsodakaṃ vā madhukodakaṃ vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         āmodbhavāṃ bilvavacāyutais tu jayet kaṣāyairatha <ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>dīpanīyaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.48.29"><label>ut.48.29</label> āmrātabhallātabalāyutāni pibet
                        kaṣāyāṇyatha dīpanāni |
                        <caesura/>
                         gurvannajātāṃ vamanairjayecca kṣayādṛte sarvakṛtāṃ ca tṛṣṇām || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.48.30"><label>ut.48.30</label> śramodbhavāṃ māṃsaraso nihanti
                        guḍodakaṃ vāpyathavāpi manthaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhaktoparodhāttṛṣito yavāgūmuṣṇāṃ piben manthamatho himaṃ ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.48.31"><label>ut.48.31</label> yā snehapītasya bhavecca tṛṣṇā
                        tatroṣṇamambhaḥ prapiben manuṣyaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         madyodbhavāmardhajalaṃ nihanti madyaṃ tṛṣāṃ yāpi ca madyapasya || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.48.32"><label>ut.48.32</label>
                        <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>tṛṣṇodbhavāṃ hanti
                        jalaṃ suśītaṃ saśarkaraṃ sekṣurasaṃ tathāmbhaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         svaiḥ svaiḥ kaṣāyairvamanāni tāsāṃ tathā jvaroktāni ca pācanāni || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.48.33"><label>ut.48.33</label> lepāvagāhau pariṣecanāni
                        kuryāttathā śītagṛhāṇi cāpi |
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃśodhanaṃ kṣīrarasau ghṛtāni sarvāsu lehānmadhurān himāṃś ca ||</l>


                    <trailer>iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kāyacikitsātantre (daśamo
                        'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) aṣṭacatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||48 ||</trailer>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.49.8"><label>ut.49.8</label>

                        <caesura/>
                         pūrvarūpaṃ mataṃ chardyā yathāsvaṃ ca vibhāvayet || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.49.9"><label>ut.49.9</label>
                        <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>pracchardayet

                        <caesura/>
                         śrāntaḥ saghoṣaṃ bahuśaḥ kaṣāyaṃ jīrṇe 'dhikaṃ sānilajā vamis tu || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.49.10"><label>ut.49.10</label> yo 'mlaṃ bhṛśaṃ vā
                        kaṭutiktavaktraḥ pītaṃ saraktaṃ haritaṃ vamedvā |
                        <caesura/>
                         sadāhacoṣajvaravaktraśoṣo mūrcchānvitaḥ<ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref> pittanimittajā sā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.49.11"><label>ut.49.11</label> yo hṛṣṭaromā madhuraṃ prabhūtaṃ

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.49.12"><label>ut.49.12</label> sarvāṇi rūpāṇi bhavanti yasyāṃ sā

                        <caesura/>
                         bībhatsajā dauhṛdajāmajā ca <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.49.13"><label>ut.49.13</label> śūlahṛllāsabahulā<ref

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.49.15"><label>ut.49.15</label> āmāśayotkleśabhavā hi

                <div n="50" type="level2" subtype="adhyāyaḥ">
                    <head>pañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
                    <l xml:id="Su.6.50.1"><label>ut.50.1</label> athāto hikkāpratiṣedhaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.50.2"><label>ut.50.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.50.3"><label>ut.50.3</label> vidāhiguruviṣṭambhir
                        ūkṣābhiṣyandibhojanaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śītapānāsanasthānarajodhūmānilānalaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.50.4"><label>ut.50.4</label>
                        vyāyāmakarmabhārādhvavegāghātāpatarpaṇaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         āmadoṣābhighātastrīkṣayadoṣaprapīḍanaiḥ<ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref> || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.50.5"><label>ut.50.5</label> viṣamāśanādhyanaśanais tathā
                        samaśanair api |
                        <caesura/>
                         hikkā śvāsaś ca kāsaś ca nṛṇāṃ samupajāyate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.50.6"><label>ut.50.6</label> muhurmuhurvāyurudeti sasvano
                        yakṛtplihāntrāṇi mukhādivākṣipan |
                        <caesura/>
                         sa ghoṣavānāśu hinastyasūn yatastatas tu hikketi bhiṣagbhir ucyate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.50.7"><label>ut.50.7</label> annajāṃ yamalāṃ kṣudrāṃ gambhīrāṃ
                        mahatīṃ tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         vāyuḥ kaphenānugataḥ pañca hikkāḥ karoti hi || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.50.8"><label>ut.50.8</label> mukhaṃ kaṣāyamaratirgauravaṃ
                        kaṇṭhavakṣasoḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pūrvarūpāṇi hikkānāmāṭopo jaṭharasya ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.50.9"><label>ut.50.9</label> tvaramāṇasya cāhāraṃ
                        bhuñjānasyāthavā ghanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         vāyurannairavastīrṇaḥ kaṭukairardito bhṛśam<ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref> || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.50.10"><label>ut.50.10</label> hikkayatyūrdhvago bhūtvā tāṃ
                        vidyādannajāṃ bhiṣak |
                        <caesura/>
                         cireṇa yamalairvegairyā hikkā saṃpravartate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.50.11"><label>ut.50.11</label> kampayantī śirogrīvaṃ yamalāṃ tāṃ
                        vinirdiśet |
                        <caesura/>
                         vikṛṣṭakālairyā vegairmandaiḥ samabhivartate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.50.12"><label>ut.50.12</label> kṣudrikā nāma sā hikkā jatrumūlāt
                        pradhāvitā |
                        <caesura/>
                         nābhipravṛttā yā hikkā ghorā gambhīranādinī || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.50.13"><label>ut.50.13</label>
                        śuṣkauṣṭhakaṇṭhajihvāsyaśvāsapārśvarujākarī |
                        <caesura/>
                         anekopadravayutā gambhīrā nāma sā smṛtā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.50.14"><label>ut.50.14</label> marmāṇyāpīḍayantīva satataṃ yā
                        pravartate |
                        <caesura/>
                         dehamāyamya vegena ghoṣayatyatitṛṣyataḥ<ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref> |
                        <caesura/>
                         mahāhikketi sā jñeyā sarvagātraprakampinī || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.50.15"><label>ut.50.15</label> āyamyate hikkato 'ṅgāni yasya
                        dṛṣṭiś cordhvaṃ tāmyate yasya gāḍham |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣīṇo 'nnadviṭ <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>kāsate
                        yaś ca hikkī tau dvāvantyau varjayed dhikkamānau || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.50.16"><label>ut.50.16</label> prāṇāyāmodvejanatrāsanāni
                        sūcītodaiḥ saṃbhramaś cātra śastaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yaṣṭyāhvaṃ vā mākṣikeṇāvapīḍe pippalyo vā śarkarācūrṇayuktāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.50.17"><label>ut.50.17</label> sarpiḥ koṣṇaṃ kṣīramikṣo raso vā
                        nātikṣīṇe chardanaṃ <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                        >&#x2020;</ref>śāntihetoḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         nārīpayaḥpiṣṭamaśuklacandanaṃ ghṛtaṃ sukhoṣṇaṃ ca sasaindhavaṃ tathā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.50.18"><label>ut.50.18</label> cūrṇīkṛtaṃ saindhavamambhasāthavā
                        nihanti hikkāṃ ca hitaṃ ca nasyataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yuñjyāddhūmaṃ śālaniryāsajātaṃ naipālaṃ vā goviṣāṇodbhavaṃ vā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.50.19"><label>ut.50.19</label> sarpiḥsnigdhaiś carmabālaiḥ kṛtaṃ
                        vā hikkāsthāne svedanaṃ cāpi kāryam |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣaudropetaṃ gairikaṃ kāñcanāhvaṃ lihyādbhasma grāmyasattvāsthijaṃ vā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.50.20"><label>ut.50.20</label>
                        tadvacchvāvinmeṣagośalyakānāṃ(gośallakānāṃ) romāṇyantardhūmadagdhāni cātra |
                        <caesura/>
                         madhvājyāktaṃ barhipatraprasūtamevaṃ bhasmaudumbaraṃ tailvakaṃ vā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.50.21"><label>ut.50.21</label> svarjikṣāraṃ bījapūrādrasena
                        kṣaudropetaṃ hanti līḍhvāśu hikkām |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarpiḥsnigdhā ghnanti hikkāṃ yavāgvaḥ koṣṇagrāsāḥ pāyaso vā sukhoṣṇaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.50.22"><label>ut.50.22</label> śuṇṭhītoye sādhitaṃ kṣīramājaṃ
                        tadvat pītaṃ śarkarāsaṃyutaṃ vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         ātṛptervā sevyamānaṃ nihantyād ghrātaṃ hikkāmāśu mūtraṃ tvajāvyoḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.50.23"><label>ut.50.23</label> sapūtikīṭaṃ
                            laśunogragandhāhiṅgvabjamācūrṇya<ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                            >&#x2020;</ref> subhāvitaṃ tat |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣaudraṃ sitāṃ vāraṇakeśaraṃ ca pibedrasenekṣumadhūkajena || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.50.24"><label>ut.50.24</label> pibet palaṃ vā lavaṇottamasya
                        dvābhyāṃ palābhyāṃ haviṣaḥ samagram |
                        <caesura/>
                         harītakīṃ koṣṇajalānupānāṃ pibedghṛtaṃ kṣāramadhūpapannam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.50.25"><label>ut.50.25</label> rasaṃ kapitthānmadhupippalībhyāṃ
                            <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>śuktipramāṇaṃ
                        prapibet sukhāya || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.50.26"><label>ut.50.26</label> kṛṣṇāṃ sitāṃ cāmalakaṃ ca līḍhaṃ
                        saśṛṅgaveraṃ madhunāthavāpi |
                        <caesura/>
                         kolāsthimajjāñjanalājacūrṇaṃ hikkā nihanyānmadhunāvalīḍham || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.50.27"><label>ut.50.27</label> pāṭalāyāḥ phalaṃ puṣpaṃ gairikaṃ
                        kaṭurohiṇī |
                        <caesura/>
                         kharjūramadhyaṃ māgadhyaḥ kāśīśaṃ dadhināma ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.50.28"><label>ut.50.28</label> catvāra ete yogāḥ syuḥ
                        pratipādapradarśitāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         madhudvitīyāḥ kartavyāste hikkāsu vijānatā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.50.29"><label>ut.50.29</label>
                        kapotapārāvatalāvaśaka(lla)śvadaṃṣṭragodhāvṛṣadaṃśajān rasān |
                        <caesura/>
                         pibet phalāmlānahimān sasaindhavān snigdhāṃstathaivarṣyamṛgadvijodbhavān || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.50.30"><label>ut.50.30</label> virecanaṃ pathyatamaṃ
                        sasaindhavaṃ ghṛtaṃ sukhoṣṇaṃ ca sitopalāyutam |
                        <caesura/>
                         sadāgatāvūrdhvagate 'nuvāsanaṃ vadanti kecicca hitāya hikkinām ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.51.1"><label>ut.51.1</label> athātaḥ śvāsapratiṣedhaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.51.3"><label>ut.51.3</label> yaireva kāraṇairhikkā bahubhiḥ
                        saṃpravartate |
                        <caesura/>
                         taireva kāraṇaiḥ śvāso ghoro bhavati dehinām || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.51.4"><label>ut.51.4</label> vihāya prakṛtiṃ vāyuḥ prāṇo 'tha
                        kaphasaṃyutaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śvāsayatyūrdhvago bhūtvā taṃ śvāsaṃ paricakṣate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.51.5"><label>ut.51.5</label> kṣudrakastamakaś chinno
                        mahānūrdhvaś ca pañcadhā |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhidyate sa mahāvyādhiḥ śvāsa eko viśeṣataḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.51.6"><label>ut.51.6</label> prāgrūpaṃ tasya hṛtpīḍā bhaktadveṣo
                        'ratiḥ parā |
                        <caesura/>
                         ānāhaḥ pārśvayoḥ śūlaṃ vairasyaṃ vadanasya ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.51.7"><label>ut.51.7</label> kiñcidārabhamāṇasya yasya śvāsaḥ
                        pravartate |
                        <caesura/>
                         niṣaṇṇasyaiti śāntiṃ ca sa kṣudra iti saṃjñitaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.51.8"><label>ut.51.8</label> tṛṭsvedavamathuprāyaḥ
                        kaṇṭhaghurghurikānvitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         viśeṣāddurdine tāmyec chvāsaḥ sa tamako mataḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.51.9"><label>ut.51.9</label> ghoṣeṇa mahatāviṣṭaḥ sakāsaḥ
                        sakapho naraḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yaḥ śvasityabalo 'nnadviṭ <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                            >&#x2020;</ref>suptastamakapīḍitaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.51.10"><label>ut.51.10</label> sa śāmyati kaphe hīne svapataś ca
                        vidhardhate |
                        <caesura/>
                         mūrcchājvarābhibhūtasya jñeyaḥ pratamakas tu saḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.51.11"><label>ut.51.11</label> ādhmāto dahyamānena bastinā

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.51.12"><label>ut.51.12</label> niḥsaṃjñaḥ pārśvaśūlārtaḥ
                        śuṣkakaṇṭho 'tighoṣavān |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.51.13"><label>ut.51.13</label> marmasvāyamyamāneṣu śvasanmūḍho

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.51.49"><label>ut.51.49</label> khastho vilayanaṃ yāti mārutaś ca

                        caiva bhojayitvā rasaudanam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.51.50"><label>ut.51.50</label> vātaśleṣmavibandhe vā bhiṣag
                        dhūmaṃ prayojayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         manaḥśilādevadāruharidrācchadanāmiṣaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.51.51"><label>ut.51.51</label> lākṣorubūkamūlaiś ca kṛtvā vartīr
                        vidhānataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                        <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                        >&#x2020;</ref>sarpiryavamadhūcchiṣṭaśālaniryāsajaṃ tathā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.51.52"><label>ut.51.52</label> śṛṅgabālakhurasnāyutvak samastaṃ
                        gavām api |
                        <caesura/>
                         turuṣkaśallakīnāṃ ca gugguloḥ padmakasya ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.51.53"><label>ut.51.53</label> ete sarve sasarpiṣkā dhūmāḥ kāryā
                        vijānatā |
                        <caesura/>
                         balīyasi kaphagraste vamanaṃ savirecanam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.51.54"><label>ut.51.54</label> durbale caiva rūkṣe ca tarpaṇaṃ
                        hitamucyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         jāṅgalorabhrajairmāṃsairānūpair vā susaṃskṛtaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.51.55"><label>ut.51.55</label> nidigdhikāṃ cāmalakapramāṇāṃ
                        hiṅgvardhayuktāṃ madhunā suyuktām |
                        <caesura/>
                         lihannaraḥ śvāsanipīḍito hi śvāsaṃ jayatyeva balāttryaheṇa || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.51.56"><label>ut.51.56</label> yathāgniriddhaḥ <ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>pavanānuviddho vajraṃ
                        yathā vā surarājamuktam |
                        <caesura/>
                         rogāstathaite khalu durnivārāḥ śvāsaś ca kāsaś ca vilambikā ca ||</l>

                <div n="53" type="level2" subtype="adhyāyaḥ">
                    <head>tripañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
                    <l xml:id="Su.6.53.1"><label>ut.53.1</label> athātaḥ
                        svarabhedapratiṣedhamadhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.53.2"><label>ut.53.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.53.3"><label>ut.53.3</label>
                            atyuccabhāṣaṇaviṣādhyayanātigītaśītādibhiḥ<ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref> prakupitāḥ pavanādayas
                        tu |
                        <caesura/>
                         srotaḥsu te svaravaheṣu gatāḥ pratiṣṭhāṃ hanyuḥ svaraṃ bhavati cāpi hi
                        ṣaḍvidhaḥ saḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.53.4"><label>ut.53.4</label> vātena kṛṣṇanayanānanamūtravarcā
                        bhinnaṃ śanairvadati gadgadavat svaraṃ ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         pittena pītavadanākṣipurīṣamūtro brūyād galena <ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>paridāhasamanvitena || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.53.5"><label>ut.53.5</label> kṛcchrāt kaphena satataṃ
                        kapharuddhakaṇṭho mandaṃ śanairvadati cāpi divā viśeṣaḥ<ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref> |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvātmake bhavati sarvavikārasaṃpadavyaktatā ca vacasastamasādhyamāhuḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.53.6"><label>ut.53.6</label> dhūpyeta vāk kṣayakṛte
                        kṣayamāpnuyāc ca vāgeṣa cāpi(vāpi) hatavāk parivarjanīyaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                        <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>antargalaṃ
                        svaramalakṣyapadaṃ cireṇa <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                            >&#x2020;</ref>medaś cayādvadati digdhagalauṣṭhatāluḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.53.7"><label>ut.53.7</label> kṣīṇasya vṛddhasya kṛśasya cāpi
                        cirotthito yaś ca sahopajātaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         medasvinaḥ sarvasamudbhavaś ca svarāmayo yo na sa siddhimeti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.53.8"><label>ut.53.8</label> snigdhān
                        svarāturanarānapakṛṣṭadoṣān nyāyena <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                            >&#x2020;</ref>tān vamanarecanabastibhiś ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         nasyāvapīḍamukhadhāvanadhūmalehaiḥ saṃpādayecca vividhaiḥ kavalagrahaiś ca
                        || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.53.9"><label>ut.53.9</label> yaḥ śvāsakāsavidhirādita eva
                        coktastaṃ cāpy aśeṣamavatārayituṃ yateta |
                        <caesura/>
                         vaiśeṣikaṃ ca vidhimūrdhvamato vadāmi taṃ vai svarāturahitaṃ nikhilaṃ
                        nibodha || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.53.10"><label>ut.53.10</label> svaropaghāte 'nilaje bhuktopari
                        ghṛtaṃ pibet |
                        <caesura/>
                         kāsamardakavātārkamārkavasvarase śṛtam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.53.11"><label>ut.53.11</label> pītaṃ ghṛtaṃ hantyanilaṃ
                        siddhamārtagale rase |
                        <caesura/>
                         yavakṣārājamodābhyāṃ citrakāmalakeṣu vā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.53.12"><label>ut.53.12</label> devadārvagnikābhyāṃ vā
                        siddhāmājaṃ samākṣikam |
                        <caesura/>
                         sukhodakānupāno vā sasarpiṣko guḍaudanaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.53.13"><label>ut.53.13</label> kṣīrānupānaṃ pitte tu pibet
                        sarpiratandritaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         aśnīyāc ca sasarpiṣkaṃ yaṣṭīmadhukapāyasam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.53.14"><label>ut.53.14</label> lihyānmadhurakāṇāṃ vā cūrṇaṃ
                        madhughṛtāplutam |
                        <caesura/>
                         śatāvarīcūrṇayogaṃ balācūrṇamathāpi vā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.53.15"><label>ut.53.15</label> pibet kaṭūni mūtreṇa kaphaje
                        svarasaṃkṣaye |
                        <caesura/>
                         lihyādvā madhutailābhyāṃ bhuktvā khādet kaṭūni vā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.53.16"><label>ut.53.16</label> svaropaghāte medoje
                        kaphavadvidhiriṣyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvaje kṣayaje cāpi pratyākhyāyācaret kriyām || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.53.17"><label>ut.53.17</label> śarkarāmadhumiśrāṇi śṛtāni
                        madhuraiḥ saha |
                        <caesura/>
                         pibet payāṃsi yasyoccairvadato 'bhihataḥ svaraḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.57.4"><label>ut.57.4</label> hṛcchūlapīḍanayutaṃ virasānanatvaṃ

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.57.5"><label>ut.57.5</label> kaṇḍūgutvakaphasaṃsravasādatandrāḥ

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.57.6"><label>ut.57.6</label> saṃrāgaśokabhayaviplutacetasastu

                        <caesura/>

                        cūrṇam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.57.7"><label>ut.57.7</label>
                        kṛṣṇāviḍaṅgayavabhasmahareṇubhārgīrāsnailahiṅgulavaṇottamanāgarāṇām |
                        <caesura/>

                        sasaindhavasitāmadhusarpiriṣṭaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.57.8"><label>ut.57.8</label> nimbāmbuvāmitavataḥ kaphaje
                        'nupānaṃ rājadrumāmbu madhunā tu sadīpyakaṃ syāt |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.57.9"><label>ut.57.9</label>
                        drākṣāpaṭolaviḍavetrakarīranimbamūrvābhayākṣabadarāmalakendravṛkṣaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>

                        yathāvat || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.57.10"><label>ut.57.10</label> mustāṃ vacāṃ trikaṭukaṃ
                        rajanīdvayaṃ ca bhārgīṃ ca kuṣṭhamatha nirdahanīṃ ca piṣṭvā |
                        <caesura/>
                         mūtre 'vije dviradamūtrayute pacedvā pāṭhāṃ tugāmativiṣāṃ rajanīṃ ca
                        mukhyām || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.57.11"><label>ut.57.11</label> maṇḍūkimarkamamṛtāṃ ca

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.57.12"><label>ut.57.12</label> sātmyān <ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>svadeśaracitān
                        vividhāṃś ca bhakṣyān pānāni mūlaphalaṣāḍavarāgayogān |
                        <caesura/>
                         adyādrasāṃś ca vividhān vividhaiḥ prakārairbhuñjīta cāpi
                        laghurūkṣamanaḥsukhāni || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.57.13"><label>ut.57.13</label> āsthāpanaṃ vidhivadatra virecanaṃ
                        ca kuryānmṛdūni śirasaś ca virecanāni |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.57.14"><label>ut.57.14</label> kṣaudrāyutāni
                            vitarenmukhabodhanārthamanyāni<ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                            >&#x2020;</ref> tiktakaṭukāni ca bheṣajāni |
                        <caesura/>
                         mustādirājataruvargadaśāṅgasiddhaiḥ kvāthairjayenmadhuyutairvividhaiś ca
                        lehaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.57.15"><label>ut.57.15</label> mūtrāsavairguḍakṛtaiś ca tathā
                        tvariṣṭaiḥ kṣārāsavaiś ca madhumādhavatulyagandhaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         syādeṣa eva kaphavātahate vidhiś ca śāntiṃ gate hutabhuji praśamāya tasya
                        || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.57.16"><label>ut.57.16</label> icchābhighātabhayaśokahate
                        'ntaragnau bhāvān bhavāya vitaret khalu śakyarūpān |
                        <caesura/>
                         artheṣu <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>cāpy
                        apaciteṣu punarbhavāya paurāṇikaiḥ śrutiśatairanumānayettam<ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref> || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.57.17"><label>ut.57.17</label> dainyaṃ gate manasi bodhanamatra
                        śastaṃ yadyat priyaṃ tadupasevyamarocake tu ||</l>


                    <trailer>iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kāyacikitsātantre
                        'rocakapratiṣedho nāma (ekonaviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) saptapañcāśattamo
                        'dhyāyaḥ ||57 ||</trailer>

                    <head>ūnaṣaṣṭitamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
                    <l xml:id="Su.6.59.1"><label>ut.59.1</label> athāto
                        mūtrakṛcchrapratiṣedhamadhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.59.2"><label>ut.59.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.59.3"><label>ut.59.3</label> vātena pittena kaphena sarvais
                        tathā+ābhighātaiḥ śakṛdaśmarībhyām |
                        <caesura/>
                         tathāparaḥ śarkarayā sukaṣṭo mūtropaghātaḥ kathito 'ṣṭamas tu || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.59.4"><label>ut.59.4</label> alpamalpaṃ samutpīḍya
                        muṣkamehanabastibhiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         phaladbhir iva kṛcchreṇa vātāghātena mehati || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.59.5"><label>ut.59.5</label> hāridramuṣṇaṃ raktaṃ vā
                        muṣkamehanabastibhiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         agninā dahyamānābhaiḥ pittāghātena mehati || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.59.6"><label>ut.59.6</label> snigdhaṃ śuklamanuṣṇaṃ ca
                        muṣkamehanabastibhiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃhṛṣṭaromā gurubhiḥ śleṣmāghātena mehati || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.59.7"><label>ut.59.7</label> dāhaśītarujāviṣṭo nānāvarṇaṃ
                        muhurmuhuḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tāmyamānas tu kṛcchreṇa sannipātena mehati || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.59.8"><label>ut.59.8</label> mūtravāhiṣu śalyena
                        kṣateṣvabhihateṣu ca |
                        <caesura/>

                            rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref> || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.59.9"><label>ut.59.9</label> vātabastes tu tulyāni tasya liṅgāni
                        lakṣayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         śakṛtas tu pratīghātādvāyurviguṇatāṃ gataḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.59.10"><label>ut.59.10</label> ādhmānaṃ ca saśūlaṃ ca
                        mūtrasaṅgaṃ karoti hi |
                        <caesura/>
                         aśmarīhetukaḥ pūrvaṃ mūtraghāta udāhṛtaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.59.11"><label>ut.59.11</label> aśmarī śarkarā caiva <ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>tulye saṃbhavalakṣaṇaiḥ
                        |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.59.12"><label>ut.59.12</label> pacyamānasya pittena
                        bhidyamānasya vāyunā |
                        <caesura/>
                         śleṣmaṇo 'vayavā bhinnāḥ śarkarā iti saṃjñitāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.59.13"><label>ut.59.13</label> hṛtpīḍā vepathuḥ śūlaṃ kukṣau<ref

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.59.16"><label>ut.59.16</label> aśmarīṃ ca samāśritya yaduktaṃ
                        prasamīkṣya tat |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathādoṣaṃ prayuñjīta snehādim api ca kramam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.59.17"><label>ut.59.17</label> śvadaṃṣṭrāśmabhidau kumbhīṃ
                        hapuṣāṃ kaṇṭakārikām |
                        <caesura/>
                         balāṃ śatāvarīṃ rāsnāṃ varuṇaṃ girikarṇikām || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.59.18"><label>ut.59.18</label> tathā vidārigandhādiṃ saṃhṛtya
                        traivṛtaṃ pacet |
                        <caesura/>
                         tailaṃ ghṛtaṃ vā tat peyaṃ tena vāpyanuvāsanam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.59.19"><label>ut.59.19</label> dadyāduttarabastiṃ ca
                        vātakṛcchropaśāntaye |
                        <caesura/>
                         śvadaṃṣṭrāsvarase tailaṃ saguḍakṣīranāgaram || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.59.20"><label>ut.59.20</label> paktvā tat pūrvavadyojyaṃ
                        tatrānilarujāpaham |
                        <caesura/>
                         tṛṇotpalādikākolīnyagrodhādigaṇaiḥ kṛtam(śṛtam) || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.59.21"><label>ut.59.21</label> pītaṃ ghṛtaṃ pittakṛcchraṃ
                        nāśayet kṣīrameva vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         dadyāduttarabastiṃ ca pittakṛcchropaśāntaye || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.59.22"><label>ut.59.22</label> ebhir eva kṛtaḥ snehastrividheṣv
                        api bastiṣu |
                        <caesura/>
                         hitaṃ virecanaṃ cekṣukṣīradrākṣārasairyutam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.59.23"><label>ut.59.23</label> surasoṣakamustādau varuṇādau ca
                            <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>yat kṛtam |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.59.24"><label>ut.59.24</label> yathādoṣocchrayaṃ kuryād etāneva
                        ca sarvaje |
                        <caesura/>
                         phalguvṛś cīradarbhāśmasāracūrṇaṃ ca vāriṇā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.59.25"><label>ut.59.25</label> surekṣurasadarbhāmbupītaṃ
                        kṛcchrarujāpaham |
                        <caesura/>
                         tathābhighātaje kuryāt sadyovraṇacikitsitam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.59.26"><label>ut.59.26</label> mūtrakṛcchre śakṛjjāte kāryā
                        vātaharī kriyā |
                        <caesura/>
                         svedāvagāhāvabhyaṅgabasticūrṇakriyāstathā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.59.27"><label>ut.59.27</label> ye tvanye tu tathā kṛcchre tayoḥ
                        proktaḥ kriyāvidhiḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.60.7"><label>ut.60.7</label> devāstathā śatrugaṇāś ca teṣāṃ

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.60.9"><label>ut.60.9</label> saṃsvedī dvijagurudevadoṣavaktā

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.60.12"><label>ut.60.12</label> pretebhyo visṛjati saṃstareṣu

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.60.13"><label>ut.60.13</label> bhūmau yaḥ prasarati sarpavat

                        <caesura/>
                         khyātaṃ phalaghṛtaṃ strīṇāṃ vandhyānāṃ cāśu garbhadam ||) </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.62.30"><label>ut.62.30</label> brahmīmaindrīṃ viḍaṅgāni vyoṣaṃ
                        hiṅgu surāṃ jaṭhām |
                        <caesura/>
                         viṣaghnīṃ laśunaṃ rāsnāṃ viśalyāṃ surasāṃ vacām || </l>

                        <caesura/>

                            >&#x2020;</ref>gajamūtreṇa peṣayet || </l>

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.62.34"><label>ut.62.34</label> śāntadoṣaṃ viśuddhaṃ ca

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.64.45"><label>ut.64.45</label> śṛtena payasā rātrau
                        śarkarāmadhureṇa ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         pratyagrakusumākīrṇe śayane harmyasaṃsthite || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.64.46"><label>ut.64.46</label> śayīta candanārdrāṅgaḥ spṛśyamāno
                        'nilaiḥ sukhaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tāpātyaye hitā nityaṃ rasā ye guravastrayaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.64.47"><label>ut.64.47</label> payo māṃsarasāḥ koṣṇāstailāni ca

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.64.48"><label>ut.64.48</label> nidāghopacitaṃ caiva prakupyantaṃ
                        samīraṇam |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.64.49"><label>ut.64.49</label> (nadījalaṃ rūkṣamuṣṇamudamanthaṃ

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.64.50"><label>ut.64.50</label> navānnarūkṣaśītāmbusaktūṃś cāpi

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.64.51"><label>ut.64.51</label> harmyamadhye nivāte ca bhajec

                        viṣopamam |

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.64.55"><label>ut.64.55</label> kupitaṃ śamayed vāyuṃ vārṣikaṃ

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.64.56"><label>ut.64.56</label> ghorānṛtukṛtān rogānnāpnoti sa

                        || </l>

                        raktapittaviṣāturān |
                        <caesura/>

                        kevalamevauṣadhamupayujyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.65.1"><label>ut.65.1</label> athātas tantrayuktim adhyāyaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.65.3"><label>ut.65.3</label> dvātriṃśattatantrayuktayo bhavanti
                        śāstre |
                        <caesura/>
                         tadyathā adhikaraṇaṃ, yogaḥ, padārthaḥ, hetvarthaḥ, uddeśaḥ, nirdeśaḥ,
                        upadeśaḥ, apadeśaḥ, pradeśaḥ, atideśaḥ, apavarjaḥ, vākyaśeṣaḥ, arthāpattiḥ,
                        viparyayaḥ, prasaṅgaḥ, ekāntaḥ, anekāntaḥ, pūrvapakṣaḥ, nirṇayaḥ, anumataṃ,
                        vidhānam, anāgatāvekṣaṇam, atikrāntāvekṣaṇaṃ, saṃśayaḥ, vyākhyānaṃ,
                        svasaṃjñā, nirvacanaṃ, nidarśanaṃ, niyogaḥ, vikalpaḥ, samuccayaḥ, ūhyam, iti
                        || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.65.4"><label>ut.65.4</label> atrāsāṃ tantrayuktīnāṃ kiṃ
                        prayojanam ucyate vākyayojanamarthayojanaṃ ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.65.5"><label>ut.65.5</label> bhavanti cātra ślokāḥ

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.65.8"><label>ut.65.8</label> tatra yam artham adhikṛtyocyate
                        tad adhikaraṇaṃ; yathā rasaṃ doṣaṃ vā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.65.9"><label>ut.65.9</label> yena vākyaṃ yujyate sa yogaḥ |
                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>
                         siddhaṃ balābhyāṃ ca sadevadāru hitāya nityaṃ galagaṇḍaroge |
                        <caesura/>
                         ityatra tailaṃ siddhaṃ pibediti prathamaṃ vaktavye tṛtīyapāde siddhamiti
                        prayuktaṃ, evaṃ dūrasthānām api padānāmekīkaraṇaṃ yogaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.65.10"><label>ut.65.10</label> yo 'rtho 'bhihitaḥ sūtre pade
                            <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>vā sa padārthaḥ;
                        padasya padayoḥ padānāṃ vārthaḥ padārthaḥ; aparimitāś ca padārthāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā snehasvedāñjaneṣu nirdiṣṭeṣu dvayostrayāṇāṃ
                        vārthānāmupapattirdṛśyate, tatra yo 'rthaḥ pūrvāparayogasiddho bhavati sa
                        grahītavyaḥ; yathā devotpattimadhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāma ityukte sandihyate
                        buddhiḥ katamasya <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                        >&#x2020;</ref>vedasyotpattiṃ vakṣyatīti, yataḥ ṛgvedādayas tu vedāḥ; vida
                        vicāraṇe, vidḷ lābhe, ity etayoś ca dhātvoranekārthayoḥ prayogāt,tatra
                        pūrvāparayogamupalabhya pratipattirbhavati āyurvedotpattimayaṃ vivakṣuriti;
                        eṣa padārthaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.65.11"><label>ut.65.11</label>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.65.22"><label>ut.65.22</label> prakaraṇāntareṇa <ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>samāpanaṃ prasaṅgaḥ,

                        vedotpattāvabhidhāya, bhūtacintāyāṃ punaruktaṃ yato 'bhihitaṃ
                        pañcamahābhūtaśarīrisamavāyaḥ puruṣa iti, sa khalveṣa
                        karmapuruṣaś cikitsādhikṛta iti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.65.23"><label>ut.65.23</label> (<ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>sarvatra)

                        so 'nekāntaḥ |

                        kecid vipākam iti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.65.25"><label>ut.65.25</label> ākṣepapūrvakaḥ praśnaḥ

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.65.26"><label>ut.65.26</label> tasyottaraṃ nirṇayaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā śarīraṃ prapīḍya paś cād adho gatvā vasāmedomajjānuviddhaṃ mūtraṃ
                        visṛjati vātaḥ, evam asādhyā vātajā iti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.65.27"><label>ut.65.27</label> tathā coktam kṛtsnaṃ śarīraṃ
                        niṣpīḍya medomajjāvasāyutaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         adhaḥ prakupyate vāyustenāsādhyās tu vātajāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.65.28"><label>ut.65.28</label> paramatamapratiṣiddham anumatam |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā anyo brūyāt sapta rasā iti, taccāpratiṣedhād anumanyate kathaṃcid iti
                        || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.65.29"><label>ut.65.29</label> prakaraṇānupūrvyābhihitaṃ
                        vidhānam |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā sakthimarmāṇyekādaśa prakaraṇānupūrvyābhihitāni || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.65.30"><label>ut.65.30</label> evaṃ vakṣyatītyanāgatāvekṣaṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā ślokasthāne brūyāt cikitsiteṣu vakṣyāmīti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.65.31"><label>ut.65.31</label> yatpūrvamuktaṃ
                        tadatikrāntāvekṣaṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā cikitsiteṣu brūyāt ślokasthāne yadīritam iti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.65.32"><label>ut.65.32</label> ubhayahetudarśanaṃ saṃśayaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                        <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>yathā
                        talahṛdayābhighātaḥ prāṇaharaḥ, pāṇipādacchedanamaprāṇaharam iti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.65.33"><label>ut.65.33</label> tantre 'tiśayopavarṇanaṃ
                        vyākhyānam |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā iha pañcaviṃśatikaḥ puruṣo vyākhyāyate, anyeṣvāyurvedatantreṣu
                        bhūtādiprabhṛtyārabhya <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                            >&#x2020;</ref>cintā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.65.34"><label>ut.65.34</label> anyaśāstrāsāmānyā svasaṃjñā |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā mithunam iti madhusarpiṣorgrahaṇaṃ; lokaprasiddhamudāharaṇaṃ <ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>vā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.65.35"><label>ut.65.35</label> niś citaṃ vacanaṃ nirvacanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā āyurvidyate 'sminnanena vā āyurvindatītyāyurvedaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.65.36"><label>ut.65.36</label>
                        <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                        >&#x2020;</ref>dṛṣṭāntavyaktir nidarśanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā agnir vāyunā sahitaḥ <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                            >&#x2020;</ref>kakṣe vṛddhiṃ gacchati tathā vātapittakaphaduṣṭo vraṇa
                        iti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.65.37"><label>ut.65.37</label> idam eva kartavyam iti niyogaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā pathyameva bhoktavyam iti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.65.38"><label>ut.65.38</label> idaṃ cedaṃ ceti samuccayaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā māṃsavarge eṇahariṇādayo lāvatittiriśāraṅgāś ca pradhānānīti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.65.39"><label>ut.65.39</label> idaṃ vedaṃ ceti vikalpaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā rasaudanaḥ saghṛtā yavāgūrvā (bhavatviti) || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.65.40"><label>ut.65.40</label> yadanirdiṣṭaṃ buddhyā<ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>+avagamyate tadūhyam |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā abhihitam annapānavidhau caturvidhaṃ cānnam upadiśyate bhakṣyaṃ bhojyaṃ
                        lehyaṃ peyamiti, evaṃ caturvidhe vaktavye dvividham abhihitam; idam atrohyam
                        annapāne viśiṣṭayor dvayor grahaṇe kṛte caturṇām api grahaṇaṃ bhavatīti;
                            <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>caturvidhaś
                        cāhāraḥ praviralaḥ, prāyeṇa dvividha eva; ato dvitvaṃ prasiddham iti |
                        <caesura/>
                         kiñcānyat annena bhakṣyam avaruddhaṃ, ghanasādharmyāt; peyena lehyaṃ,
                            dravasādhamyāt<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref> || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.65.41"><label>ut.65.41</label> bhavanti cātra <ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>sāmānyadarśanenāsāṃ
                        vyavasthā saṃpradarśitā |
                        <caesura/>
                         viśeṣas tu yathāyogam upadhāryo vipaś citā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.65.42"><label>ut.65.42</label> dvātriṃśadyuktayo hy etās
                        tantrasāragaveṣaṇe |
                        <caesura/>
                         mayā samyag vinihitāḥ śabdārthanyāyasaṃyutāḥ<ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref> || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.65.43"><label>ut.65.43</label> yo hy etā vidhivad vetti
                        dīpībhūtās tu buddhimān |
                        <caesura/>
                         sa pūjārho bhiṣakśreṣṭha iti dhanvantarer matam ||</l>


                    <trailer>iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantre tantrabhūṣaṇādhyāyeṣu
                        tantrayuktir nāma (tṛtīyo 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) pañcaṣaṣṭitamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||65
                        ||</trailer>

                        <caesura/>
                         chinnaśāstrārthasaṃdehaṃ sūkṣmāgādhāgamodadhim | </l>

                    <l/>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.66.4"><label>ut.66.4</label> viśvāmitrasutaḥ śrīmān suśrutaḥ
                        paripṛcchati |
                        <caesura/>
                         dviṣaṣṭirdoṣabhedā ye purastātparikīrtitāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.66.5"><label>ut.66.5</label> kati tatraikaśo jñeyā dviśo
                        vāpy athavā triśaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā saṃśayacchinmahātapāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.66.6"><label>ut.66.6</label> prītātmā nṛpaśārdūlaḥ<ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref> suśrutāyāha tattvataḥ
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         trayo doṣā dhātavaś ca purīṣaṃ mūtram eva ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.66.7"><label>ut.66.7</label> dehaṃ sandhārayanty ete hy avyāpannā
                        rasair hitaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         puruṣaḥ ṣoḍaśakalaḥ prāṇāś caikādaśaiva ye || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.66.8"><label>ut.66.8</label> rogāṇāṃ tu sahasraṃ yac chataṃ
                        viṃśatir eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                        <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>śataṃ ca pañca
                        dravyāṇāṃ trisaptatyadhikottaram || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.66.9"><label>ut.66.9</label> vyāsataḥ kīrtitaṃ taddhi bhinnā
                        doṣāstrayo guṇāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         dviṣaṣṭidhā bhavanty ete bhūyiṣṭham iti niś cayaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.66.10"><label>ut.66.10</label> traya eva pṛthak doṣā dviśo nava
                        samādhikaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         trayodaśādhikaikadvisamam adhyolbaṇais triśaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.66.11"><label>ut.66.11</label> pañcāśadevaṃ tu saha bhavanti
                        kṣayamāgataiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                        <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                        >&#x2020;</ref>kṣīṇamadhyādhikakṣīṇakṣīṇavṛddhais tathāparaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.66.12"><label>ut.66.12</label> dvādaśaivaṃ samākhyātāstrayo doṣā
                        dviṣaṣṭidhā |
                        <caesura/>
                         miśrā dhātumalairdoṣā yānty asaṃkhyeyatāṃ punaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.66.13"><label>ut.66.13</label> tasmāt prasaṅgaṃ saṃyamya
                        doṣabhedavikalpanaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         rogaṃ viditvopacared rasabhedair yathair itaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.66.14"><label>ut.66.14</label> bhiṣak kartātha karaṇaṃ rasā
                        doṣās tu kāraṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         kāryam ārogyam evaikam anārogyam ato 'nyathā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.66.15"><label>ut.66.15</label> adhyāyānāṃ tu ṣaṭṣaṣṭyā
                        grathitārthapadakramam |
                        <caesura/>
                        evam etad aśeṣeṇa tantram uttaram ṛddhimat || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.66.16"><label>ut.66.16</label> spaṣṭagūḍhārthavijñānam agāḍham
                        andacetasām |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathāvidhi yathāpraśnaṃ bhavatāṃ parikīrtitam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="Su.6.66.17"><label>ut.66.17</label> sahottaraṃ tv etad adhītya sarvaṃ
                        brāhmaṃ vidhānena yathoditena |
                        <caesura/>
                         na hīyate 'rthān manaso 'bhyupetād etad vaco brahmam atīvasatyam ||</l>
